Mahāparinirvāṇasūtra

Wal 1.1 evaṁ mayā śrutam ||

Wal 1.2 ekaṁ samayaṁ bhagavān rājagṛhe viharati gṛdhrakūṭe parvate || tena khalu samayena rājā māgadho ’jātaśatrur vaidehīputro vṛjibhiḥ sārdhaṁ prativiruddhaḥ ||

Wal 1.3 sa evaṁ pariṣadi vācaṁ bhāṣate || aham imān vṛjīn ṛddhāṁś ca sphītāṁś ca kṣemāṁś ca subhikṣāṁś cākīrṇabahujanamanuṣyāṁś cotsādayiṣyāmi vināśayiṣyāmy anayena vyasanam āpādayiṣyāmi ||

Wal 1.4 atha rājā māgadho ’jātaśatrur vaidehīputro varṣākāraṁ brāhmaṇamagadhamahāmātram āmantrayate ||

Wal 1.5 ehi tvaṁ varṣākāra yena bhagavāṁs tenopasaṁkrama || upetyāsmākaṁ vacanena bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vandasvālpābādhatāṁ ca pṛcchālpātaṅkatāṁ ca laghūtthānatāṁ ca yātrāṁ ca balaṁ ca sukhaṁ cānavadyatāṁ ca sparśavihāratāṁ ca ||

Wal 1.6 evaṁ ca vada || rājā māgadho ’jātaśatrur vaidehīputro vṛjibhiḥ sārdhaṁ prativiruddhaḥ || sa evaṁ pariṣadi vācaṁ bhāṣate || aham imān vṛjīn ṛddhāṁś ca sphītāṁś ca kṣemāṁś ca subhikṣāṁś cākīrṇabahujanamanuṣyāṁś cotsādayiṣyāmi vināśayiṣyāmy anayena vyasanam āpādayiṣyāmi ||

Wal 1.7 kiṁ bhagavān āmantrayate || yathā varṣākāra sa bhagavāṁ vyākaroti tathaivodgṛhāṇa || tat kasmād dhetoḥ || avitathāvādino hi bhavanti tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksaṁbuddhāḥ ||

Wal 1.8 evaṁ deveti varṣākāro brāhmaṇamagadhamahāmātro rājño māgadhasyājātaśatror vaidehīputrasya pratiśrutya sarvaśvetaṁ vaḍabāratham abhiruhya … māṇavagaṇaparivṛtaḥ sauvarṇena daṇḍakama … rājagṛhān niryāti bhagavato ’ntikenopadarśanāya bhagavantaṁ paryupāsanāyai || tasya yāvad yānasya bhūmis tāvad yānena gatvā yānād avatīrya padbhyām eva gṛdhrakūṭaṁ parvatam abhiruhya yena bhagavāṁs tenopajagāmopetya bhagavatā sārdhaṁ saṁmukhaṁ saṁmodanīṁ saṁraṁjanīṁ vividhāṁ kathāṁ vyatisāryaikānte nyaṣīdat |

Wal 1.9 ekānte niṣaṇṇo varṣākāro brāhmaṇamagadhamāhāmātro bhagavantam idam avocat ||

Wal 1.10 rājā māgadho ’jātaśatrur vaidehīputro bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vandaty alpābādhatāṁ ca pṛcchaty alpātaṅkatāṁ ca pūrvavad yāvat sparśavihāratāṁ ca ||

Wal 1.11 sukhī bhavatu varṣākāra rājā māgadho ’jātaśatrur vaidehīputras tvaṁ ca ||

Wal 1.12 rājā bhadanta māgadho ’jātaśatrur vaidehīputro vṛjibhiḥ sārdhaṁ prativiruddhaḥ || sa evaṁ pariṣadi vācaṁ bhāṣate || aham imān vṛjīn ṛddhāṁś ca sphītāṁś ca kṣemāṁś ca subhikṣāṁś cākīrṇabahujanamanuṣyāṁś cotsādayiṣyāmi vināśayiṣyāmy anayena vyasanam āpādayiṣyāmi ||

Wal 1.13 kiṁ bhagavāṅ gautama āmantrayate ||

Wal 1.14 ekam ahaṁ varṣākāra samayaṁ vṛjiṣu janapadeṣu viharāmi cāpāle caitye || tatra mayā vṛjīnāṁ saptāparihāṇīyā dharmā deśitāḥ || yāvac ca varṣākāra vṛjaya imān saptāparihāṇīyān dharmān samādāya vartiṣyante vṛjiṣu ca saptāparihāṇīyā dharmāḥ sandrakṣyante vṛddhir eva vṛjīnāṁ pratikāṁkṣitavyā kuśalānāṁ dharmāṇāṁ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 1.15 evam ahaṁ bhadantāsya bhagavato gautamasya saṁkṣiptena bhāṣitasyāvibhaktasya vistareṇārthaṁ nājānāmi || bhagavān gautamo saṁkṣiptena bhāṣitasyārthaṁ vibhaktaṁ vistareṇa bhāṣeta || evam ahaṁ bhagavato gautamasya saṁkṣiptena bhāṣitasyāvibhaktaṁ vistareṇārthaṁ sādhu evājñāsyāmi ||

Wal 1.16 tena khalu samayenāyuṣmān ānando bhagavataḥ pṛṣṭhataḥ sthito bhagavantaṁ vījayamānaḥ || tatra bhagavān āyuṣmantam ānandam āmantrayate ||

Wal 1.17 kiṁ nu tvayānanda śrutaṁ vṛjayo ’bhīkṣṇasannipātā abhīkṣṇaṁ sannipātabahulā viharanti ||

Wal 1.18 śrutaṁ me bhadanta vṛjayo ’bhīkṣṇasannipātā abhīkṣṇaṁ sannipātabahulā viharanti ||

Wal 1.19 yāvac ca varṣākāra vṛjayo ’bhīkṣṇasannipātā abhīkṣṇaṁ sannipātabahulā vihariṣyanti vṛddhir eva vṛjīnāṁ pratikāṁkṣitavyā kuśalānāṁ dharmāṇāṁ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 1.20 kiṁ nu tvayānanda śrutaṁ vṛjayaḥ samagrāḥ sannipatanti samagrā vyuttiṣṭhanti samagrā vṛjikaraṇīyāni kurvanti ||

Wal 1.21 śrutaṁ me bhadanta vṛjayaḥ samagrāḥ sannipatanti samagrā vyuttiṣṭhanti samagrā vṛjikaraṇīyāni kurvanti ||

Wal 1.22 yāvac ca varṣākāra vṛjayaḥ samagrāḥ sannipatiṣyanti samagrā vyutthāsyanti samagrā vṛjikaraṇīyāni kariṣyanti vṛddhir eva vṛjīnāṁ pratikāṁkṣitavyā kuśalānāṁ dharmāṇāṁ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 1.23 kiṁ nu tvayānanda śrutaṁ vṛjayo ’praṇihitaṁ na praṇidadhati praṇihitaṁ ca na samucchindati yathāprajñaptaṁ vṛjidharmaṁ samādāya vartante ||

Wal 1.24 śrutaṁ me bhadanta vṛjayo ’praṇihitaṁ na praṇidadhati praṇihitaṁ ca na samucchindanti yathāprajñaptaṁ vṛjidharmaṁ samādāya vartante ||

Wal 1.25 yāvac ca varṣākāra vṛjayo ’praṇihitaṁ na praṇidhāsyanti praṇihitaṁ ca na samucchetsyanti yathāprajñaptaṁ vṛjidharmaṁ samādāya vartiṣyante vṛddhir eva vṛjīnāṁ pratikāṁkṣitavyā kuśalānāṁ dharmāṇāṁ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 1.26 kiṁ nu tvayānanda śrutaṁ yās tā vṛjīnāṁ vṛjiprajāpatyo vṛjikumārikāś ca pitṛrakṣitā mātṛrakṣitā bhrātṛrakṣitā bhaginīrakṣitāḥ śvaśurarakṣitā śvaśrurakṣitā jñātirakṣitā gotrarakṣitāḥ saparidaṇḍāḥ sasvāmikāḥ kanyāḥ paraparigṛhītā antaśo mālāguṇaparikṣiptā api tadrūpāsu na sahasā balenānupraskandya kāmeṣu cāritram āpadyante ||

Wal 1.27 śrutaṁ me bhadanta vṛjayo yās tā vṛjīnāṁ vṛjiprajāpatyo vṛjikumārikāś ca pitṛrakṣitā mātṛrakṣitā pūrvavad yāvad antaśo mālāguṇaparikṣiptā api tadrūpāsu na sahasā balenānupraskandya kāmeṣu cāritram āpadyante ||

Wal 1.28 yāvac ca varṣākāra vṛjayo yās tā vṛjīnāṁ vṛjiprajāpatyo vṛjikumārikāś ca pūrvavad yāvad antaśo mālāguṇaparikṣiptā api tadrūpāsu na sahasā balenānupraskandya kāmeṣu cāritram āpatsyante vṛddhir eva vṛjīnāṁ pratikāṁkṣitavyā kuśalānāṁ dharmāṇāṁ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 1.29 kiṁ nu tvayānanda śrutaṁ vṛjayo ye te vṛjīnāṁ vṛjimahallakās tān satkurvanti gurukurvanti mānayanti pūjayanti teṣāṁ vacanaṁ śrotavyaṁ manyante ||

Wal 1.30 śrutaṁ me bhadanta vṛjayo ye te vṛjīnāṁ vṛjimahallakās tān satkurvanti gurukurvanti mānayanti pūjayanti teṣāṁ vacanaṁ śrotavyaṁ manyante ||

Wal 1.31 yāvac ca varṣākāra vṛjayo ye te vṛjīnāṁ vṛjimahallakās tān satkariṣyanti gurukariṣyanti mānayiṣyanti pūjayiṣyanti teṣāṁ vacanaṁ śrotavyaṁ maṁsyante vṛddhir eva vṛjīnāṁ pratikāṁkṣitavyā kuśalānāṁ dharmāṇāṁ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 1.32 kiṁ nu tvayānanda śrutaṁ vṛjayo ye te vṛjīnāṁ caturdikṣu vṛjicaityās tān satkurvanti gurukurvanti mānayanti pūjayanti teṣāṁ ca paurāṇaṁ cihnavṛttaṁ na samucchindanti ||

Wal 1.33 śrutaṁ me bhadanta vṛjayo ye te vṛjīnāṁ caturdikṣu vṛjicaityās tān satkurvanti gurukurvanti mānayanti pūjayanti teṣāṁ ca paurāṇaṁ cihnavṛttaṁ na samucchindanti ||

Wal 1.34 yāvac ca varṣākāra vṛjayo ye te vṛjīnāṁ caturdikṣu vṛjicaityās tān satkariṣyanti gurukariṣyanti mānayiṣyanti pūjayiṣyanti teṣāṁ ca paurāṇaṁ cihnavṛttaṁ na samucchetsyanti vṛddhir eva vṛjīnāṁ pratikāṁkṣitavyā kuśalānāṁ dharmāṇāṁ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 1.35 kiṁ nu tvayānanda śrutaṁ vṛjīnām arhatām antike tīvracetasa ārakṣāsmṛtiḥ pratyupasthitā kaccid anāgatāś cārhanta āgaccheyur āgatāś cābhirameraṁs te ca na vihanyerañ cīvarapiṇḍapātaśayanāsanaglānapratyayabhaiṣajyapariṣkāraiḥ ||

Wal 1.36 śrutaṁ me bhadanta vṛjīnām arhatām antike tīvracetasa ārakṣāsmṛtiḥ pratyupasthitā kaccid anāgatāś cārhanta āgaccheyur āgatāś cābhirameraṁs te ca na vihanyerañ cīvarapiṇḍapātaśayanāsanaglānapratyayabhaiṣajyapariṣkāraiḥ ||

Wal 1.37 yāvac ca varṣākāra vṛjīnām arhatām antike tīvracetasa ārakṣāsmṛtiḥ pratyupasthitā bhaviṣyati kaccid anāgatāś cārhanta āgaccheyur āgatāś cābhirameraṁs te ca na vihanyerañ cīvarapiṇḍapātaśayanāsanaglānapratyayabhaiṣajyapariṣkārair vṛddhir eva vṛjīnāṁ pratikāṁkṣitavyā kuśalānāṁ dharmāṇāṁ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 1.38 yāvac ca varṣākāra vṛjaya imān saptāparihāṇīyān dharmān samādāya vartiṣyante vṛjiṣu ca saptāparihāṇīyā dharmāḥ sandrakṣyante vṛddhir eva vṛjīnāṁ pratikāṁkṣitavyā kuśalānāṁ dharmāṇāṁ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 1.39

Wal 1.40 ekaikena tāvad bho gautamāṅgena samanvāgatā vṛjayo ’gamanīyāḥ syū rājño māgadhasyājātaśatror vaidehīputrasya kaḥ punar vādaḥ sarvaiḥ ||

Wal 1.41 hanta bho gautama gamiṣyāmo bahukṛtyāḥ smo bahukaraṇīyāḥ ||

Wal 1.42 yasyedānīṁ varṣākāra kālaṁ manyase ||

Wal 1.43 atha varṣākāro brāhmaṇamagadhamahāmātro bhagavato bhāṣitam abhinandyānumodya bhagavato ’ntikāt prakrāntaḥ ||

Wal 2.1 tatra bhagavān āyuṣmantam ānandam āmantrayate || yāvanto bhikṣavo gṛdhrakūṭaparvatam upaniśritya viharanti tān sarvān upasthānaśālāyāṁ sannipātaya ||

Wal 2.2 evaṁ bhadantety āyuṣmān ānando bhagavataḥ pratiśrutya yāvanto bhikṣavo gṛdhrakūṭaṁ parvatam upaniśritya viharanti tān sarvān upasthānaśālāyāṁ sannipātayitvā yena bhagavāṁs tenopajagāma || upetya bhagavatpādau śirasā vanditvaikānte ’sthāt || ekāntasthita āyuṣmān ānando bhagavantam idam avocat ||

Wal 2.3 yāvanto bhadanta bhikṣavo gṛdhrakūṭaṁ parvatam upaniśritya viharanti te sarva upasthānaśālāyāṁ sannipatitāḥ || yasyedānīṁ bhagavāṅ kālaṁ manyate ||

Wal 2.4 atha bhagavān yenopasthānaśālā tenopajagāma || upetya purastād bhikṣusaṁghasya prajñapta evāsane nyaṣīdat || niṣadya bhagavān bhikṣūn āmantrayate sma ||

Wal 2.5 saptāhaṁ vo bhikṣavo ’parihāṇīyān dharmān deśayiṣyāmi tāñ śṛṇuta sādhu ca suṣṭhu ca manasi kuruta bhāṣiṣye || saptāparihāṇīyā dharmāḥ katame ||

Wal 2.6 yāvac ca bhikṣavo ’bhīkṣṇasannipātā abhīkṣṇaṁ sannipātabahulā vihariṣyanti vṛddhir eva bhikṣūṇāṁ pratikāṁkṣitavyā kuśalānāṁ dharmāṇāṁ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 2.7 yāvac ca bhikṣavaḥ samagrāḥ sannipatiṣyanti samagrā vyutthāsyanti samagrāḥ saṁghakaraṇīyāni kariṣyanti vṛddhir eva bhikṣūṇāṁ pratikāṁkṣitavyā kuśalānāṁ dharmāṇāṁ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 2.8 yāvac ca bhikṣavo ’praṇihitaṁ na praṇidhāsyanti praṇihitaṁ ca na samucchetsyanti yathāprajñaptikāṁ śikṣāṁ samādāya vartiṣyante vṛddhir eva bhikṣūṇāṁ pratikāṁkṣitavyā kuśalānāṁ dharmāṇāṁ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 2.9 yāvac ca bhikṣavas tṛṣṇāyāḥ paunarbhavikyā nandirāgasahagatāyās tatra tatrābhinandinyā vaśaṁ na gacchanti vṛddhir eva bhikṣūṇāṁ pratikāṁkṣitavyā kuśalānāṁ dharmāṇāṁ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 2.10 yāvac ca bhikṣavo ye te bhikṣavaḥ sthavirā rātrijñāś cirapravrajitā … tān satkariṣyanti gurukariṣyanti mānayiṣyanti pūjayiṣyanti teṣāṁ vacanaṁ śrotavyaṁ maṁsyante vṛddhir eva bhikṣūṇāṁ pratikāṁkṣitavyā kuśalānāṁ dharmāṇāṁ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 2.11 yāvac ca bhikṣavo ’raṇyavanaprasthāni prāntāni śayanāsanāny adhyāvasiṣyanti vṛddhir eva bhikṣūṇāṁ pratikāṁkṣitavyā kuśalānāṁ dharmāṇāṁ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 2.12 yāvac ca bhikṣavaḥ sabrahmacāriṇām antike tīvracetasa ārakṣāsmṛtiḥ pratyupasthitā kaccid anāgatāś ca sabrahmacāriṇa āgaccheyur āgatāś cābhirameraṁs te ca na vihanyerañ cīvarapiṇḍapātaśayanāsanaglānapratyayabhaiṣajyapariṣkārair vṛddhir eva bhikṣūṇāṁ pratikāṁkṣitavyā kuśalānāṁ dharmāṇāṁ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 2.13 yāvac ca bhikṣava imān saptāparihāṇīyān dharmān samādāya vartiṣyante bhikṣuṣu ca saptāparihāṇīyā dharmāḥ sandrakṣyante vṛddhir eva bhikṣūṇāṁ pratikāṁkṣitavyā kuśalānāṁ dharmāṇāṁ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 2.14 aparān api saptāparihāṇīyān dharmān deśayiṣyāmi tāñ śṛṇuta sādhu ca suṣṭhu ca manasi kuruta bhāṣiṣye || saptāparihāṇīyā dharmāḥ katame ||

Wal 2.15 yāvac ca bhikṣavaḥ śāstāraṁ satkariṣyanti gurukariṣyanti mānayiṣyanti pūjayiṣyanti śāstāraṁ satkṛtvā gurukṛtvā mānayitvā pūjayitvopaśritya vihariṣyanti dharmaṁ śikṣām anuśāsanam apramādaṁ pratisaṁstaraṁ samādhiṁ satkariṣyanti gurukariṣyanti mānayiṣyanti pūjayiṣyanti samādhiṁ satkṛtvā gurukṛtvā mānayitvā pūjayitvopaśritya vihariṣyanti vṛddhir eva bhikṣūṇāṁ pratikāṁkṣitavyā kuśalānāṁ dharmāṇāṁ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 2.16 Nur im Tib.

Wal 2.17 aparān api saptāparihāṇīyān dharmān deśayiṣyāmi tāñ śṛṇuta sādhu ca suṣṭhu ca manasi kuruta bhāṣiṣye || saptāparihāṇīyā dharmāḥ katame ||

Wal 2.18 yāvac ca bhikṣavo na karmārāmā bhaviṣyanti na bhāṣyārāmā na nidrārāmā na saṁgaṇikārāmā … viśeṣādhigamenāntarāvasān … vṛddhir eva bhikṣūṇāṁ pratikāṁkṣitavyā kuśalānāṁ dharmāṇāṁ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 2.19 Nur im Tib.

Wal 2.20 aparān api saptāparihāṇīyān dharmān deśayiṣyāmi tāñ śṛṇuta sādhu ca suṣṭhu ca manasi kuruta bhāṣiṣye || saptāparihāṇīyā dharmāḥ katame ||

Wal 2.21 yāvac ca bhikṣavaḥ śrāddhā bhaviṣyanti hrīmanto bhaviṣyanty avatrāpiṇa ārabdhavīryā upasthitasmṛtayaḥ samāhitāḥ prajñāvanto bhaviṣyanti vṛddhir eva bhikṣūṇāṁ pratikāṁkṣitavyā kuśalānāṁ dharmāṇāṁ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 2.22 Nur im Tib.

Wal 2.23 aparān api saptāparihāṇīyān dharmān deśayiṣyāmi tāñ śṛṇuta sādhu ca suṣṭhu ca manasi kuruta bhāṣiṣye || saptāparihāṇīyā dharmāḥ katame ||

Wal 2.24 yāvac ca bhikṣavo dharmajñā arthajñāḥ kālajñā mātrajñā ātmajñāḥ pariṣajjñāḥ pudgalavarāvarajñā vṛddhir eva bhikṣūṇāṁ pratikāṁkṣitavyā kuśalānāṁ dharmāṇāṁ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 2.25 Nur im Tib.

Wal 2.26 aparān api saptāparihāṇīyān dharmān deśayiṣyāmi tāñ śṛṇuta sādhu ca suṣṭhu ca manasi kuruta bhāṣiṣye || saptāparihāṇīyā dharmāḥ katame ||

Wal 2.27 yāvac ca bhikṣavaḥ smṛtisaṁbodhyaṅgaṁ bhāvayiṣyanti vivekaniśritaṁ virāganiśritaṁ nirodhaniśritaṁ vyavasargapariṇataṁ dharmavicayavīryaprītiprasrabdhisamādhyupekṣāsaṁbodhyaṅgaṁ bhāvayiṣyanti vivekaniśritaṁ virāganiśritaṁ nirodhaniśritaṁ vyavasargapariṇataṁ vṛddhir eva bhikṣūṇāṁ pratikāṁkṣitavyā kuśalānāṁ dharmāṇāṁ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 2.28 yāvac ca bhikṣava imān saptāparihāṇīyān dharmān samādāya vartiṣyante bhikṣuṣu ca saptāparihāṇīyā dharmāḥ sandrakṣyante vṛddhir eva bhikṣūṇāṁ pratikāṁkṣitavyā kuśalānāṁ dharmāṇāṁ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 2.29 ṣaḍ ahaṁ vo bhikṣavaḥ saṁraṁjanīyān dharmān deśayiṣyāmi tāñ śṛṇuta sādhu ca suṣṭhu ca manasi kuruta bhāṣiṣye || ṣaṭ saṁraṁjanīyā dharmāḥ katame ||

Wal 2.30 maitraṁ me kāyakarma pratyupasthitaṁ bhaviṣyati śāstur antike vijñānāñ ca sabrahmacāriṇām || ayaṁ dharmaḥ saṁraṁjanīyaḥ priyakaraṇo gurukaraṇo manāpakaraṇaḥ priyatvāya gurutvāya gauravāya bhāvanāya saṁgrahāya samādhaye ’vigrahāyāvivādāya ekotībhāvāya saṁvartate ||

Wal 2.31 maitraṁ vākkarma

Wal 2.32 maitraṁ manaskarma

Wal 2.33 ye te lābhā dhārmikā dharmalabdhā antataḥ pātragatāḥ pātraparyāpannās tadrūpeṣu lābheṣu sādhāraṇaparibhojino bhaviṣyāmo ’pratiguptabhojinaḥ sārdhaṁ vijñaiḥ sabrahmacāribhiḥ ||

ayaṁ dharmaḥ saṁraṁjanīyaḥ pūrvavat ||

Wal 2.34 yāni tāni śīlāny akhaṇḍāny acchidrāṇy aśabalāny akalmāṣāṇi bhujiṣyāṇy aparāmṛṣṭāni susamāptāni susamādattāni vijñapraśastāny agarhitāni vijñais tadrūpaiḥ śīlaiḥ śīlasāmānyagatā bhaviṣyāmaḥ sārdhaṁ vijñaiḥ sabrahmacāribhiḥ || ayaṁ dharmaḥ saṁraṁjanīyaḥ pūrvavat ||

Wal 2.35 yeyaṁ dṛṣṭir āryā nairyāṇikā nairvedhikā niryāti tatkarasamyagduḥkhakṣayāya duḥkhasyāntakriyāyai tadrūpayā dṛṣṭyā dṛṣṭisāmānyagatā bhaviṣyāmaḥ sārdhaṁ vijñaiḥ sabrahmacāribhiḥ || ayaṁ dharmaḥ saṁraṁjanīyaḥ pūrvavad yāvad ekotībhāvāya saṁvartate ||

Wal 2.36 yāvac ca bhikṣava imān ṣaṭ saṁraṁjanīyān dharmān samādāya vartiṣyante bhikṣuṣu ca ṣaṭ saṁraṁjanīyā dharmāḥ sandrakṣyante vṛddhir eva bhikṣūṇāṁ pratikāṁkṣitavyā kuśalānāṁ dharmāṇāṁ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 2.37 Nur Chin.

Hier im Tib. Uddāna

Wal 3.1 tatra bhagavān āyuṣmantam ānandam āmantrayate || āgamayānanda yena pāṭaligrāmakaḥ ||

Wal 3.2 evaṁ bhadantety āyuṣmān ānando bhagavataḥ pratyaśrauṣīt || atha bhagavān sārdhaṁ bhikṣusaṁghena magadheṣu janapadeṣu caryāṁ caran antarā ca pāṭaligrāmakam antarā ca rājagṛhaṁ rājāgārake rātrīṁ viharati veṇuyaṣṭikām upaniśritya ||

Wal 3.3 atha bhagavān bhikṣūn āmantrayate sma || caturṇāṁ bhikṣava āryasatyānām ajñānād adarśanād anavabodhād aprativedhād idaṁ dīrgham adhvānaṁ saṁdhāvitaṁ saṁsṛtaṁ mayā yuṣmābhir eva ca || katameṣāṁ caturṇām ||

Wal 3.4 duḥkhasya duḥkhasamudayasya duḥkhanirodhasya duḥkhanirodhagāminyāḥ pratipado ’jñānād adarśanād anavabodhād aprativedhād idaṁ dīrgham adhvānaṁ saṁdhāvitaṁ saṁsṛtaṁ mayā yuṣmābhir eva ca ||

Wal 3.5 tad idaṁ duḥkham āryasatyam anuviddhaṁ pratividdham ucchinnā bhavanetrī vikṣīṇo jātisaṁsāro nāstīdānīṁ punarbhavaḥ ||

Wal 3.6 duḥkhasamudayo duḥkhanirodho duḥkhanirodhagāminī pratipad āryasatyam anuviddhaṁ pratividdham ucchinnā bhavanetrī vikṣīṇo jātisaṁsāro nāstīdānīṁ punarbhavaḥ ||

Wal 3.7 Nur im Tib.

Wal 3.8 caturṇām āryasatyānāṁ
yathābhūtam adarśanāt ||

saṁsṛtaṁ dīrgham adhvānaṁ
mayā yuṣmābhir eva ca | 1

Wal 3.9 tāni satyāni dṛṣṭāni
bhavanetrī samuddhṛtā ||

vikṣīṇo jātisaṁsāro
nāstīdānīṁ punarbhavaḥ | 2

Wal 4.1 tatra bhagavān āyuṣmantam ānandam āmantrayate || āgamayānanda yena pāṭaligrāmakaḥ ||

Wal 4.2 evaṁ bhadantety āyuṣmān ānando bhagavataḥ pratyaśrauṣīt || atha bhagavān magadheṣu janapadeṣu caryāṁ caran pāṭaligrāmakam anuprāptaḥ pāṭaligrāmake viharati pāṭalake caitye ||

Wal 4.3 aśrauṣuḥ pāṭaligrāmīyakā brāhmaṇagṛhapatayo bhagavān gautamo magadheṣu janapadeṣu caryāṁ caran pāṭaligrāmakam anuprāptaḥ pāṭaligrāmake viharati pāṭalake caitye ||

Wal 4.4 śrutvā ca punaḥ saṁghāt saṁghaṁ pūgāt pūgaṁ saṁgamya samāgamya pāṭaligrāmakān niṣkramya yena bhagavāṁs tenopajagmur upetya bhagavatpādau śirasā vanditvaikānte nyaṣīdan ||

Wal 4.5 ekāntaniṣaṇṇān pāṭaligrāmīyakān brāhmaṇagṛhapatīn bhagavān idam avocat ||

Wal 4.6 pañceme brāhmaṇagṛhapataya ādīnavāḥ pramāde || katame pañca ||

Wal 4.7 iha brāhmaṇagṛhapatayaḥ pramattaḥ pramādādhikaraṇahetor mahatīṁ bhogajyāniṁ nigacchati || yad brāhmaṇagṛhapatayaḥ pramattaḥ pramādādhikaraṇahetor mahatīṁ bhogajyāniṁ nigacchati || ayaṁ prathama ādīnavaḥ pramāde ||

Wal 4.8 punar aparaṁ brāhmaṇagṛhapatayaḥ pramattaḥ pramādādhikaraṇahetor yāṁ yām eva pariṣadam upasaṁkrāmati yadi vā kṣatriyapariṣadaṁ yadi vā brāhmaṇapariṣadaṁ yadi vā gṛhapatipariṣadaṁ yadi vā śramaṇapariṣadaṁ tatra tatra madgur upasaṁkrāmaty anudagro ’viśāradaḥ || yad brāhmaṇagṛhapatayaḥ pramattaḥ pramādādhikaraṇahetor yāṁ yām eva pariṣadam upasaṁkrāmati pūrvavad yāvad aviśāradaḥ || ayaṁ dvitīya ādīnavaḥ pramāde ||

Wal 4.9 punar aparaṁ brāhmaṇagṛhapatayaḥ pramattasya pramādādhikaraṇahetor digvidikṣu pāpako ’varṇo ’kīrtiśabdaśloko ’bhyudgacchati || yad brāhmaṇagṛhapatayaḥ pramattasya pramādādhikaraṇahetor digvidikṣu pāpako ’varṇo ’kīrtiśabdaśloko ’bhyudgacchati || ayaṁ tṛtīya ādīnavaḥ pramāde ||

Wal 4.10 punar aparaṁ brāhmaṇagṛhapatayaḥ pramattaḥ pramādādhikaraṇahetor vipratisārī kālaṁ karoti || yad brāhmaṇagṛhapatayaḥ pramattaḥ pramādādhikaraṇahetor vipratisārī kālaṁ karoti || ayaṁ caturtha ādīnavaḥ pramāde ||

Wal 4.11 punar aparaṁ brāhmaṇagṛhapatayaḥ pramattaḥ pramādādhikaraṇahetoḥ kāyasya bhedān narakeṣūpapadyate || yad brāhmaṇagṛhapatayaḥ pramattaḥ pramādādhikaraṇahetoḥ kāyasya bhedān narakeṣūpapadyate || ayaṁ pañcama ādīnavaḥ pramāde ||

Wal 4.12 pañca tv ime brāhmaṇagṛhapataya ānuśaṁsā apramāde || katame pañca ||

Wal 4.13 iha brāhmaṇagṛhapatayo ’pramatto ’pramādādhikaraṇahetor na mahatīṁ bhogajyāniṁ nigacchati || yad brāhmaṇagṛhapatayo ’pramatto ’pramādādhikaraṇahetor na mahatīṁ bhogajyāniṁ nigacchati || ayaṁ prathama ānuśaṁso ’pramāde ||

Wal 4.14 punar aparaṁ brāhmaṇagṛhapatayo ’pramatto ’pramādādhikaraṇahetor yāṁ yām eva pariṣadam upasaṁkrāmati yadi vā kṣatriyapariṣadaṁ yadi vā brāhmaṇapariṣadaṁ yadi vā gṛhapatipariṣadaṁ yadi vā śramaṇapariṣadaṁ tatra tatrāmadgur upasaṁkrāmaty udagro viśāradaḥ || yad brāhmaṇagṛhapatayo ’pramatto ’pramādādhikaraṇahetor yāṁ yām eva pariṣadam upasaṁkrāmati pūrvavad yāvad viśāradaḥ || ayaṁ dvitīya ānuśaṁso ’pramāde ||

Wal 4.15 punar aparaṁ brāhmaṇagṛhapatayo ’pramattasyāpramādādhikaraṇahetor digvidikṣūdāraḥ kalyāṇaḥ kīrtiśabdaśloko ’bhyudgacchati || yad brāhmaṇagṛhapatayo ’pramattasyāpramādādhikaraṇahetor digvidikṣūdāraḥ kalyāṇaḥ kīrtiśabdaśloko ’bhyudgacchati || ayaṁ tṛtīya ānuśaṁso ’pramāde ||

Wal 4.16 punar aparaṁ brāhmaṇagṛhapatayo ’pramatto ’pramādādhikaraṇahetor na vipratisārī kālaṁ karoti || yad brāhmaṇagṛhapatayo ’pramatto ’pramādādhikaraṇahetor na vipratisārī kālaṁ karoti || ayaṁ caturtha ānuśaṁso ’pramāde ||

Wal 4.17 punar aparaṁ brāhmaṇagṛhapatayo ’pramatto ’pramādādhikaraṇahetoḥ kāyasya bhedāt sugatau svargaloke deveṣūpapadyate || yad brāhmaṇagṛhapatayo ’pramatto ’pramādādhikaraṇahetoḥ kāyasya bhedāt sugatau svargaloke deveṣūpapadyate || ayaṁ pañcama ānuśaṁso ’pramāde ||

Wal 4.18 atha bhagavān pāṭaligrāmīyakān brāhmaṇagṛhapatīn dhārmyā kathayā sandarśayati samādāpayati samuttejayati saṁpraharṣayati || anekaparyāyeṇa dhārmyā kathayā sandarśayitvā samādāpayitvā samuttejayitvā saṁpraharṣayitvā tūṣṇīm abhūt ||

Wal 4.19 atha pāṭaligrāmīyakā brāhmaṇagṛhapataya utthāyāsanād ekāṁsam uttarāsaṅgaṁ kṛtvā yena bhagavāṁs tenāñjaliṁ praṇamya bhagavantam idam avocan || adhivāsayatv asmākaṁ bhagavān āvasathe rātriṁvāsāya || adhivāsayati bhagavān pāṭaligrāmīyakānāṁ brāhmaṇagṛhapatīnāṁ tūṣṇīṁbhāvena ||

Wal 4.20 atha pāṭaligrāmīyakā brāhmaṇagṛhapatayo bhagavatas tūṣṇīṁbhāvenādhivāsanāṁ viditvā bhagavatpādau śirasā vanditvā bhagavato ’ntikāt prakrāntāḥ ||

Wal 5.1 atha bhagavān aciraprakrāntān pāṭaligrāmīyakān brāhmaṇagṛhapatīn viditvā bahir āvasathasya pādau prakṣālyāvasathaṁ praviśya nyaṣīdat ||

Wal 5.2 tena samayena varṣākāro brāhmaṇamagadhamahāmātra udyuktaḥ pāṭaligrāmakaṁ nagaraṁ māpayituṁ vṛjīnāṁ pratighātārtham || tadā pāṭaligrāmake mahāśakyamahāśakyā devatā vastuni pratigṛhṇanti ||

Wal 5.3 paryaṅkam ābhujyarjuṁ kāyaṁ praṇidhāya pratimukhaṁ smṛtim upasthāpyādrākṣīd bhagavān āvasathe divāvihāropagato divyena cakṣuṣā viśuddhenātikrāntamānuṣeṇa pāṭaligrāmake mahāśakyamahāśakyā devatā vastūni pratigṛhṇanti || dṛṣṭvā ca punaḥ sāyāhne pratisaṁlayanād vyutthāyāvasathād avatīryāvasathapracchāyāyāṁ purastād bhikṣusaṁghasya prajñapta evāsane nyaṣīdat ||

Wal 5.4 niṣadya bhagavān āyuṣmantam ānandam āmantrayate ||

ka ānandodyuktaḥ pāṭaligrāmakaṁ nagaraṁ māpayitum ||

Wal 5.5 varṣākāro bhadanta brāhmaṇamagadhamahāmātra udyuktaḥ pāṭaligrāmakaṁ nagaraṁ māpayituṁ vṛjīnāṁ pratighātārtham ||

Wal 5.6 sādhu sādhv ānanda + + varṣākāro brāhmaṇamagadhamahāmātro yathā devais trāyastriṁśaiḥ sārdham + + + + + + + ||

Wal 5.7 atrāham ānandādrākṣam āvasathe divāvihāropagataḥ pāṭaligrāmake mahāśakyamahāśakyā devatā vastūni pratigṛhṇanti ||

Wal 5.8 yasminn ānanda pradeśe mahāśakyamahāśakyā devatā vastūni pratigṛhṇanti mahāśakyānāṁ manuṣyāṇāṁ tasmin pradeśe cittaṁ krāmati yaduta vāsāya ||

Wal 5.9 yasmin pradeśe madhyā devatā vastūni pratigṛhṇanti madhyānāṁ manuṣyāṇāṁ tasmin pradeśe cittaṁ krāmati yaduta vāsāya ||

Wal 5.10 yasmin pradeśe nīcā devatā vastūni pratigṛhṇanti nīcānāṁ manuṣyāṇāṁ tasmin pradeśe cittaṁ krāmati yaduta vāsāya ||

Wal 5.11 asminn ānanda pāṭaligrāmake mahāśakyamahāśakyā devatā vastūni pratigṛhṇanti || asmin pradeśe mahāśakyānāṁ manuṣyāṇāṁ cittaṁ kramiṣyati yaduta vāsāya ||

Wal 5.12 yāvad evānandāryā āvāsā āryā vyavahārā āryā vāṇir yathaitad agraṁ bhaviṣyati puṭabhedanānāṁ yaduta pāṭaliputraṁ nagaraṁ ||

Wal 5.13 tasya trayo ’ntarāyā veditavyā agnito ’py udakato ’py abhyantarato ’pi mithobhedāt ||

Wal 6.1 aśrauṣīd varṣākāro brāhmaṇamagadhamahāmātraḥ || bhagavān gautamo magadheṣu janapadeṣu caryāṁ caran pāṭaligrāmakam anuprāptaḥ pāṭaligrāmake viharati pāṭalake caitye || paryupāsate taṁ pāṭaligrāmīyakā brāhmaṇagṛhapatayaḥ ||

Wal 6.2 śrutvā ca punaḥ pāṭaligrāmakān niṣkramya yena bhagavāṁs tenopajagāma || upetya bhagavatā sārdhaṁ saṁmukhaṁ saṁmodanīṁ saṁraṁjanīṁ vividhāṁ kathāṁ vyatisāryaikānte nyaṣīdat ||

Wal 6.3 ekāntaniṣaṇṇaṁ varṣākāraṁ brāhmaṇamagadhamahāmātraṁ bhagavān dhārmyā kathayā sandarśayati samādāpayati samuttejayati saṁpraharṣayati || anekaparyāyeṇa dhārmyā kathayā sandarśayitvā samādāpayitvā samuttejayitvā saṁpraharṣayitvā tūṣṇīm abhūt ||

Wal 6.4 atha varṣākāro brāhmaṇamagadhamahāmātra utthāyāsanād ekāṁsam uttarāsaṅgaṁ kṛtvā yena bhagavāṁs tenāñjaliṁ praṇamya bhagavantam idam avocat ||

Wal 6.5 adhivāsayatu me bhavāṅ gautamaḥ śvo bhaktena sārdhaṁ bhikṣusaṁghena || adhivāsayati bhagavān varṣākārasya brāhmaṇamagadhamahāmātrasya tūṣṇīṁbhāvena ||

Wal 6.6 atha varṣākāro brāhmaṇamagadhamahāmātro bhagavatas tūṣṇīṁbhāvenādhivāsanāṁ viditvā bhagavato bhāṣitam abhinandyānumodya bhagavato ’ntikāt prakrāntaḥ ||

Wal 6.7 atha varṣākāro brāhmaṇamagadhamahāmātras tām eva rātriṁ śuciṁ praṇītaṁ khādanīyabhojanīyaṁ samudānīya kālyam evotthāyāsanakāni prajñapyodakamaṇiṁ pratiṣṭhāpya bhagavato dūtena kālam ārocayati || samayo bho gautamo sadyo bhaktaṁ yasyedānīṁ bhavāṅ gautamaḥ kālaṁ manyate ||

Wal 6.8 atha bhagavān pūrvāhṇe nivasya pātracīvaram ādāya bhikṣusaṁghaparivṛto bhikṣusaṁghapuraskṛto yena varṣākārasya brāhmaṇamagadhamahāmātrasya bhaktābhisāras tenopajagāma || upetya purastād bhikṣusaṁghasya prajñapta evāsane nyaṣīdat ||

Wal 6.9 atha varṣākāro brāhmaṇamagadhamahāmātraḥ sukhopaniṣaṇṇaṁ buddhapramukhaṁ bhikṣusaṁghaṁ viditvā śucinā praṇītena khādanīyabhojanīyena svahastaṁ santarpayati saṁpravārayati || śucinā praṇītena khādanīyabhojanīyena svahastaṁ santarpayitvā saṁpravārayitvā bhagavantaṁ bhuktavantaṁ viditvā dhautahastam apanītapātraṁ sauvarṇaṁ bhṛṅgāraṁ gṛhītvā bhagavataḥ purato ’sthāt || āyācamāna evaṁ cāha ||

Wal 6.10 ito dānād yaḥ puṇyābhiṣyandaḥ kuśalābhiṣyandaḥ sa bhavatu pāṭaliputravāstavyānāṁ devatānāṁ dīrgharātram arthāya hitāya sukhāya || teṣāñ ca nāmnā dakṣiṇām ādiśasva ||

Wal 6.11 atha bhagavān varṣākārasya brāhmaṇamagadhamahāmātrasya tad dānam anayābhyanumodanayābhyanumodate ||

Wal 6.12 yo devatāḥ pūjayati
śrāddhaḥ puruṣapudgalaḥ ||
śāstur vākyakaro bhavati
buddhair etat praśaṁsitam |

Wal 6.13 yasmin pradeśe medhāvī
vāsaṁ kalpayati paṇḍitaḥ ||
śīlavantaṁ bhojayitvā
dakṣiṇām ādiśet tataḥ |

Wal 6.14 te mānitā mānayanti
pūjitāḥ pūjayanti ca ||
athainam anukampanti
mātā putram ivaurasam ||
devānukampitappoṣaḥ
sukhī bhadrāṇi paśyati |

Wal 7.1 atha bhagavān varṣākāraṁ brāhmaṇamagadhamahāmātraṁ dhārmyā kathayā sandarśayitvā samādāpayitvā samuttejayitvā saṁpraharṣayitvotthāyāsanāt prakrāntaḥ ||

Wal 7.2 atha varṣākāro brāhmaṇamagadhamahāmātro yat tatrotsīdanadharmaṁ tat sarvaṁ visarjanadharmam iti kṛtvā bhagavantaṁ pṛṣṭhataḥ pṛṣṭhataḥ samanubaddhaḥ ||

Wal 7.3 atha varṣākārasya brāhmaṇamagadhamahāmātrasyaitad abhavat ||

yena dvāreṇa śramaṇo gautamaḥ prathamato niṣkramiṣyati tam ahaṁ gautamadvāraṁ māpayiṣyāmi yena tīrthena śramaṇo gautamaḥ prathamato nadīṁ gaṅgām uttariṣyati tam ahaṁ gautamatīrthaṁ māpayiṣyāmi ||

Wal 7.4 atha bhagavān varṣākārasya brāhmaṇamagadhamahāmātrasya cetasā cittam ājñāya paścimena dvāreṇa niṣkramyottareṇānvāvṛtto yena nadī gaṅgā ||

Wal 7.5 tena khalu samayena māgadhakā manuṣyā nadīṁ gaṅgām uttaranty api pratyuttaranty apy ekatyāḥ śalmaliphaleṣv ekatyā alābuniḥśrayaṇikābhir ekatyās tḥlabimbopanair ekatyāś chāgalakair dṛtibhiḥ ||

Wal 7.6 atha bhagavata etad abhavat || kiṁ nu nadīṁ gaṅgām asajyamānaḥ srotaso gacchāmy āho svid apārime tīre ’ntarhitaḥ pārime tīre pratitiṣṭhāmi || atha bhagavāṁs tadrūpaṁ samādhiṁ samāpanno yathā samāhite citte ’pārime tīre ’ntarhitaḥ pārime tīre pratyasthāt ||

Wal 7.7 atha varṣākāro brāhmaṇamagadhamahāmātro yena dvāreṇa bhagavān niṣkrāntas tad gautamadvāraṁ māpayati yena tīrthena bhagavān nadīṁ gaṅgām uttīrṇas tad gautamatīrthaṁ māpayati ||

Wal 7.8 athānyataro bhikṣus tasyāṁ velāyāṁ gāthāṁ babhāṣe |

Wal 7.9 ye taranti hy ārṇavaṁ saraḥ
setuṁ kṛtvā visṛjya palvalāni ||
kolaṁ hi janāḥ prabadhnate
tīrṇā medhāvino janāḥ |

Wal 7.10 uttīrṇo bhagavān buddho
brāhmaṇas tiṣṭhati sthale ||
bhikṣavaḥ parisnāyanti
kolaṁ badhnanti śrāvakāḥ |

Wal 7.11 kiṁ kuryād udapānena
āpaś cet sarvato yadi ||
chittveha mūlaṁ tṛṣṇāyāḥ
kasya paryeṣaṇāṁ caret |

Wal 8.1 tatra bhagavān āyuṣmantam ānandam āmantrayate ||

Wal 8.2 āgamyānanda yena kuṭigrāmakaḥ ||

Wal 8.3 evaṁ bhadantety āyuṣmān ānando bhagavataḥ pratyaśrauṣīt ||

Wal 8.4 atha bhagavān yena kuṭigrāmakas tena caryāṁ prakrāntaḥ || anupūrveṇa caryāñ caraṅ kuṭigrāmakam anuprāptaḥ kuṭigrāmake viharaty uttareṇa grāmasya śiṁśapāvane ||

Wal 8.5 tatra bhagavān bhikṣūn āmantrayate ||

Wal 8.6 itīmāni bhikṣavaḥ śīlāny ayaṁ samādhir iyaṁ prajñā || śīlaparibhāvitaḥ samādhiś cirasthitiko bhavati || prajñāparibhāvitaṁ cittaṁ samyag eva vimucyate rāgadveṣamohebhyaḥ ||

Wal 8.7 evaṁ samyaksuvimuktacitta āryaśrāvakaḥ samyag eva prajānāti || kṣīṇā me jātir uṣitaṁ brahmacaryaṁ kṛtaṁ karaṇīyaṁ nāparam asmād bhavaṁ prajānāmi ||

Wal 9.1 tatra bhagavān āyuṣmantam ānandam āmantrayate ||

Wal 9.2 āgamayānanda yena nādikā ||

Wal 9.3 evaṁ bhadantety āyuṣmān ānando bhagavataḥ pratyaśrauṣīt ||

Wal 9.4 atha bhagavān vṛjiṣu janapadeṣu caryāñ caran nādikām anuprāpto nādikāyāṁ viharati kuñjikāvasathe ||

Wal 9.5 tena samayena nādikāyā mahato janakāyasya māry utthitābhūt || tathā hi karkaṭaka upāsakaḥ kālagataḥ ||

Wal 9.6 nikaṭa upāsakaḥ kaḍaṅgaraḥ kātyarṣabhaś cārur upacārur ariṣṭa upāriṣṭo bhadraḥ subhadro yaśo yaśodatto yaśottaro ’pi kālagataḥ ||

Wal 9.7 atha saṁbahulā bhikṣavaḥ pūrvāhṇe nivasya pātracīvaram ādāya nādikāṁ piṇḍāya prāvikṣan ||

Wal 9.8 aśrauṣuḥ saṁbahulā bhikṣavo nādikāṁ piṇḍāya carantaḥ || asyāṁ nādikāyāṁ mahāñ janakāyo mṛtaḥ || tathā hi karkaṭaka upāsakaḥ kālagato nikaṭo kaḍaṅgaraḥ kātyarṣabhaś cārur upacārur ariṣṭa upāriṣṭo bhadraḥ subhadro yaśo yaśodatto yaśottaraḥ kālagataḥ ||

Wal 9.9 śrutvā ca punar nādikāṁ piṇḍāya caritvā kṛtabhaktakṛtyāḥ paścādbhaktapiṇḍapātāḥ pratikrāntāḥ || pātracīvaraṁ pratiśāmya pādau prakṣālya yena bhagavāṁs tenopajagmuḥ || upetya bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvaikānte nyaṣīdan ||

Wal 9.10 ekānte niṣaṇṇāḥ saṁbahulā bhikṣavo bhagavantam idam avocan ||

Wal 9.11 iha vayaṁ bhadanta saṁbahulā bhikṣavaḥ pūrvāhṇe nivasya pātracīvaram ādāya nādikāṁ piṇḍāya prāviśāma || aśrauṣma vayam asyāṁ nādikāyāṁ karkaṭaka upāsakaḥ kālagataḥ pūrvavad yāvad yaśodatto yaśottaraḥ kālagataḥ teṣāṁ bhadanta kā gatiḥ kopapattiḥ ko ’bhisaṁparāyaḥ ||

Wal 9.12 karkaṭaka upāsakaḥ pañcānām avarabhāgīyānāṁ saṁyojanānāṁ prahāṇād aupapādukās tatra parinirvāyy anāgāmy anāvṛttidharmā punar imaṁ lokaṁ ||

Wal 9.13 nikaṭaḥ kaḍaṅgaraḥ pūrvavad yāvad yaśottara upāsakaḥ pañcānām avarabhāgīyānāṁ pūrvavad yāvat punar imaṁ lokam ||

Wal 9.14 santi bhikṣavo nādikāyām ardhatṛtīyāny upāsakaśatāni kālagatāni yāni pañcānām avarabhāgīyānāṁ saṁyojanānāṁ prahāṇād aupapādukās tatra parinirvāyiṇo ’nāgāmino ’nāvṛttidharmāṇaḥ punar imaṁ lokam ||

Wal 9.15 sātirekāṇi bhikṣavo nādikāyāṁ tryupāsakaśatāni abhyatītāni kālagatāni yāni trayāṇāṁ saṁyojanānāṁ prahāṇād rāgadveṣamohānāṁ ca tanutvāt kālaṁ kṛtvā sakṛdāgāminaḥ sakṛd imaṁ lokam āgamya duḥkhasyāntaṁ kariṣyanti ||

Wal 9.16 sātirekāṇy asyāṁ nādikāyāṁ pañcopāsakaśatāny abhyatītāni kālagatāni yāni trayāṇāṁ saṁyojanānāṁ prahāṇāc chrotaāpannā avinipātadharmāṇo niyataṁ saṁbodhiparāyaṇāḥ saptakṛtvaḥparamāḥ saptakṛtvo devāṁś ca manuṣyāṁś ca saṁdhāvya saṁsṛtya duḥkhasyāntaṁ kariṣyanti ||

Wal 9.17 kālagatāḥ kālagatā iti yūyaṁ bhikṣavas tathāgataṁ prakṣyatha viheṭhayiṣyatha tathāgataṁ na punar anena tathāgat. + + + + + + + + jātasyāvaśyaṁ kālakriyā ||

Wal 9.18 kim atrāścaryam || utpādād vā tathāgatānām anutpādād vā sthitaiveyaṁ dharmatā dharmasthitaye dhātūṁs tāṁs tathāgataḥ svayam abhijñāyābhisaṁbuddhyākhyāti prajñāpayati prasthāpayati vibhajati vivaraty uttānīkaroti deśayati saṁprakāśayati ||

Wal 9.19 yadutāsmin satīdaṁ bhavaty asyotpādād idam utpadyate yadutāvidyāpratyayāḥ saṁskārā yāvat samudayo nirodhaś ca bhavati ||

Wal 9.20

Wal 9.21 api dharmādarśaṁ nāma dharmaparyāyaṁ deśayiṣye || taṁ śṛṇuta sādhu ca suṣṭhu ca manasi kuruta bhāṣiṣye || dharmādarśo dharmaparyāyaḥ katamaḥ || buddhe dharme saṁghe ’vetyaprasādena samanvāgato bhavaty āryakāntaiḥ śīlaiḥ samanvāgato bhavati || ayam ucyate dharmādarśo dharmaparyāyaḥ || dharmādarśo dharmaparyāya iti me yad uktaṁ yuṣmākaṁ bhikṣavas tad uktam ||

Wal 9.22

Wal 10.1 tatra bhagavān āyuṣmantam ānandam āmantrayate || āgamayānanda yena vaiśālī ||

Wal 10.2 evaṁ bhadantety āyuṣmān ānando bhagavataḥ pratyaśrauṣīt ||

Wal 10.3 atha bhagavān vṛjiṣu janapadeṣu caryāṁ caran vaiśālim anuprāpto vaiśālyāṁ viharaty āmrapālivane ||

Wal 10.4 aśrauṣīd āmrapālir gaṇikā || bhagavāṅ gautamo vaiśālīm anuprāpto vaiśālyāṁ viharaty asmākam evāmravane ||

Wal 10.5 śrutvā ca punaḥ sarvālaṁkārair alaṁkṛtā strīgaṇam anvāhiṇḍayitvā bhadraṁ yānam adhiruhya vaiśālyā niryāti bhagavato ’ntikenopadarśanāya bhagavantaṁ paryupāsanāyai ||

Wal 10.6 tasyā yāvad yānabhūmis tāvad yānena gatvā yānād avatīrya padbhyām eva yena bhagavāṁs tenopasaṁkrāntā ||

Wal 10.7 adrākṣīd bhagavān anekaśatabhikṣuparivāre sanniṣaṇṇa āmrapāliṁ dūrād āgacchantīṁ dṛṣṭvā ca punar bhikṣūn āmantrayate ||

Wal 10.8 ātāpino bhikṣavo viharata saṁprajānāḥ pratismṛtāḥ || āmrapālir gaṇikātrāgatā ||

Wal 10.9 kathaṁ ca bhikṣur ātāpī bhavati ||

Wal 10.10 iha bhikṣur utpannānāṁ pāpakānām akuśalānāṁ dharmāṇāṁ prahāṇāya cchandaṁ janayati vyāyacchate vīryam ārabhate cittaṁ pragṛhṇāti pradadhāti ||

anutpannānāṁ pāpakānām akuśalānāṁ dharmāṇām anutpādāya cchandaṁ janayati pūrvavat ||

anutpannānāṁ kuśalānāṁ dharmāṇām utpādāya cchandaṁ janayati pūrvavat ||

utpannānāṁ kuśalānāṁ dharmāṇāṁ sthitaye bhūyobhāvatāyā asaṁpramoṣāya paripūraṇāya vaipulyāya cchandaṁ janayati pūrvavat || ayaṁ bhikṣur ātāpī bhavati ||

Wal 10.11 kathañ ca bhikṣuḥ saṁprajāno bhavati ||

Wal 10.12 iha bhikṣur abhikrānte pratikrānte saṁprajāno bhavaty ālokite vilokite saṁmiñjite prasārite saṁghāṭīcīvarapātradhāraṇe gate sthite niṣaṇṇe śayite jāgarite bhāṣite tūṣṇīṁbhāve supte śrame viśrame saṁprajāno bhavati || ayaṁ bhikṣur saṁprajāno bhavati ||

Wal 10.13 kathañ ca bhikṣuḥ pratismṛto bhavati ||

Wal 10.14 iha bhikṣur adhyātmaṁ kāye kāyānupaśyī viharaty ātāpī saṁprajānaḥ smṛtimān vinīyābhidhyā loke daurmanasyam || bahirdhā kāye ’dhyātmabahirdhā kāye ’dhyātmaṁ vedanāsu bahirdhā vedanāsv adhyātmabahirdhā vedanāsv adhyātmaṁ citte bahirdhā citte ’dhyātmabahirdhā citte ’dhyātmaṁ dharmeṣu bahirdhā dharmeṣv adhyātmabahirdhā dharmeṣu dharmānupaśyī viharaty ātāpī saṁprajānaḥ smṛtimān vinīyābhidhyā loke daurmanasyam || ayaṁ bhikṣuḥ pratismṛto bhavati ||

Wal 10.15 ātāpino bhikṣavo viharata saṁprajānāḥ pratismṛtāḥ || āmrapālir gaṇikātrāgatety eva mayākhyātam ||

Wal 10.16 athāmrapālir yena bhagavāṁs tenopajagāma || upetya bhagavatpādau śirasā vanditvaikānte nyaṣīdat ||

Wal 10.17 ekāntaniṣaṇṇām āmrapāliṁ bhagavān dhārmyā kathayā pūrvavad yāvat saṁpraharṣayitvā tūṣṇīm abhūt ||

Wal 10.18 atha āmrapālir utthāyāsanād yena bhagavāṁs tenāñjaliṁ praṇamya bhagavantam idam avocat ||

Wal 10.19 adhivāsayatu me bhagavāñ śvo bhaktena sārdhaṁ bhikṣusaṁghena ||

Wal 10.20 adhivāsayati bhagavāṁ tūṣṇīṁbhāvena || atha āmrapālir bhagavatas tūṣṇīṁbhāvenādhivāsanāṁ viditvā bhagavatpādau śirasā vanditvā bhagavato ’ntikāt prakrāntā ||

Wal 11.1 aśrauṣur vaiśālakā licchavayaḥ || bhagavān vṛjiṣu janapadeṣu caryāṁ caran vaiśālīm anuprāpto vaiśālyāṁ viharaty āmrapālivane ||

Wal 11.2 śrutvā pratyekapratyekaṁ bhadreṣu yāneṣv adhiruhya … māṇābhir

Wal 11.3 ekatyā nīlāśvā nīlarathā nīlapragrahapratodā nīloṣṇīṣā nīlacchatrakhaḍgakośā nīlamaṇidaṇḍakacāmarā nīlavastrālaṁkāravilepanā nīlaparivārā

Wal 11.4 ekatyāḥ pītāśvāḥ pītarathāḥ pītapragrahapratodāḥ pītoṣṇīṣāḥ pītacchatrakhaḍgakośāḥ pītamaṇidaṇḍakacāmarāḥ pītavastrālaṁkāravilepanāḥ pītaparivārā ||

Wal 11.5 ekatyā lohitāśvā lohitarathā lohitapragrahapratodā lohitoṣṇīṣā lohitacchatrakhaḍgakośā lohitamaṇidaṇḍakacāmarā lohitavastrālaṁkāravilepanā lohitaparivārā

Wal 11.6 ekatyāḥ śvetāśvāḥ śvetarathāḥ śvetapragrahapratodāḥ śvetoṣṇīṣāḥ śvetacchatrakhaḍgakośāḥ śvetamaṇidaṇḍakacāmarāḥ śvetavastrālaṁkāravilepanāḥ śvetaparivārā

Wal 11.7 uccaśabdaṁ prakṣveḍayanto mahāśabdaṁ prakṣveḍayanto vaiśālyā niṣkramya yena bhagavāṁs tenopajagmur bhagavaddarśanāya bhagavantaṁ paryupāsanāyai ||

Wal 11.8 adrākṣīd bhagavān vaiśalakāl licchavīn dūrād evāgacchato dṛṣṭvā ca punar bhikṣūn āmantrayate ||

Wal 11.9 … vaiśālakāl licchavīn paśyatha || anayarddhyā …

Wal 11.10 teṣāṁ yāvad yānabhūmis tāvad yānena gatvā yānād avatīrya padbhyām eva yena bhagavāṁs tenopajagmur upetya bhagavatpādau śirasā vanditvaikānte nyaṣīdan ||

Wal 11.11 ekāntaniṣaṇṇān vaiśālakāl licchavīn bhagavān dhārmyā kathayā sandarśayati samādāpayati samuttejayati saṁpraharṣayati ||

Wal 11.12 tena khalu samayena paiṅgiko māṇavas tasmin samāje sanniṣaṇṇo ’bhūt sannipatitaḥ || atha paiṅgiko māṇava utthāyāsanād ekāṁsaṁ cīvaraṁ kṛtvā yena bhagavāṁs tenāñjaliṁ praṇamya bhagavantam idam avocat ||

Wal 11.13 pratibhāti me bhagavan pratibhāti me sugata ||

Wal 11.14 pratibhātu te paiṅgiketi bhagavān avocat ||

Wal 11.15 atha paiṅgiko māṇavo gāthā babhāṣe ||

Wal 11.19 …

Wal 11.20 … taiḥ pañcottarāsaṅgaśatāni so …

Wal 11.21 atha bhagavān vaiśālakāl licchavīn dhārmyā kathayā sandarśayitvā samādāpayitvā samuttejayitvā saṁpraharṣayitvā tūṣṇīm abhūt ||

Wal 11.22 atha vaiśālakā licchavaya utthāyāsanād ekāṁsam uttarāsaṅgaṁ kṛtvā yena bhagavāṁs tenāñjaliṁ praṇamya bhagavantam idam avocan ||

Wal 11.23 adhivāsayatu no bhagavāñ śvo bhaktena sārdhaṁ bhikṣusaṁghena ||

Wal 11.24 nimantrito ’smi vāsiṣṭhās tatprathamata āmrapālyā ||

Wal 11.25 bhadantāmrapālyāmbakayā a … punar vayaṁ bhadantopasthāsyāmo bhagavantaṁ bhikṣusaṁghaṁ ca ||

Wal 11.26 kalyāṇam idaṁ vāsiṣṭhā uktam ||

Wal 11.27 atha vaiśālakā licchavayo bhagavato bhāṣitam abhinandyānumodya bhagavatpādau śirasā vanditvā bhagavato ’ntikāt prakrāntāḥ ||

Wal 12.1 athāmrapālis tām eva rātriṁ śuciṁ praṇītaṁ khādanīyabhojanīyaṁ samudānīya kālyam evotthāya āsanakāni prajñapyodakamaṇiṁ pratiṣṭhāpya bhagavato dūtena kālam ārocayati ||

Wal 12.2 samayo bho gautamo sadyo bhaktaṁ yasyedānīṁ bhavāṅ gautamaḥ kālaṁ manyate ||

Wal 12.3 atha bhagavān pūrvāhṇe nivasya pātracīvaram ādāya bhikṣusaṁghaparivṛto bhikṣusaṁghapuraskṛto yenāmrapālyā gaṇikāyā bhaktābhisāras tenopajagāma || upetya purastād bhikṣusaṁghasya prajñapta evāsane nyaṣīdat ||

Wal 12.4 athāmrapāliḥ sukhopaniṣaṇṇaṁ buddhapramukhaṁ bhikṣusaṁghaṁ viditvā śucinā praṇītena khādanīyabhojanīyena svahastaṁ santarpayati saṁpravārayati || śucinā praṇītena khādanīyabhojanīyena svahastaṁ santarpayitvā saṁpravārayitvā

Wal 12.5 bhagavantaṁ bhuktavantaṁ viditvā dhautahastam apanītapātraṁ nīcatarakam āsanaṁ gṛhītvā bhagavataḥ purato niṣaṇṇā dharmaśravaṇāya ||

Wal 12.6 atha bhagavān āmrapālyās tad dānam anayābhyanumodanayābhyanumodate |

Wal 12.7 dadat priyo bhavati bhajanti taṁ janāḥ
kīrtiṁ samāpnoti yaśaś ca vardhate ||
amadgubhūtaḥ pariṣadaṁ vigāhate
viśārado bhavati naro hy amatsarī |

Wal 12.8 tasmād dhi dānāni dadati paṇḍitā
vinīya mātsaryamalaṁ sukhaiṣiṇaḥ ||
te dīrgharātraṁ tridaśe pratiṣṭhitā
devānāṁ svabhāvagatā ramanti te |

Wal 12.9 kṛtāyuṣāḥ kṛtakuśalā itaś cyutāḥ
svayaṁprabhā anuvicaranti nandane ||
te tatra krīḍanti ramanti cobhayaṁ
samarpitāḥ kāmaguṇais tu pañcabhiḥ ||
śrutveha vākyam asitasya tāyinaḥ
svarge ramante sugatasya śrāvakāḥ |

Wal 12.10 atha bhagavān āmrapāliṁ dhārmyā kathayā sandarśayitvā samādāpayitvā samuttejayitvā saṁpraharṣayitvotthāyāsanāt prakrāntaḥ ||

Wal 13.1 tatra bhagavān āyuṣmantam ānandam āmantrayate ||

Wal 13.2 āgamayānanda yena veṇugrāmakaḥ ||

Wal 13.3 evaṁ bhadantety āyuṣmān ānando bhagavataḥ pratyaśrauṣīt ||

Wal 13.4 atha bhagavān vṛjiṣu janapadeṣu caryāṁ caran veṇugrāmakam anuprāpto veṇugrāmake viharaty uttareṇa grāmasya śiṁśapāvane ||

Wal 13.5 tena khalu samayena durbhikṣam abhūt kṛcchraḥ kāntāro durlabhaḥ piṇḍako yācanakena ||

Wal 13.6 tatra bhagavān bhikṣūn āmantrayate ||

Wal 13.7 etarhi bhikṣavo durbhikṣaṁ kṛcchraḥ kāntāro durlabho piṇḍako yācanakena ||

Wal 13.8 eta yūyaṁ bhikṣavo yathāsaṁstutikayā yathāsaṁlaptikayā yathāsaṁpremikayā vaiśālīsamantakena vṛjigrāmakeṣu varṣām upagacchata ||

Wal 13.9 aham apy asminn eva veṇugrāmake varṣām upagamiṣyāmy ānandena bhikṣuṇopasthāyakena || mā sarva eva piṇḍakena klāmatha ||

Wal 13.10 evaṁ bhadanteti te bhikṣavo bhagavataḥ pratiśrutya

Wal 13.11 yathāsaṁstutikayā yathāsaṁlaptikayā yathāsaṁpremikayā vaiśālīsamantakena vṛjigrāmakeṣu varṣām upagatāḥ ||

Wal 14.1 bhagavān tatraiva veṇugrāmake varṣām upagata ānandena bhikṣuṇopasthāyakena ||

Wal 14.2 tasya khalu varṣopagatasyotpannaḥ khara ābādhaḥ pragāḍhā vedanā māraṇāntikā ||

Wal 14.3 atha bhagavata etad abhavat ||

Wal 14.4 utpanno me khara ābādhaḥ pragāḍhā vedanā māraṇāntikā viprakrāntaś ca bhikṣusaṁghaḥ ||

Wal 14.5 na mama pratirūpaṁ syād yad ahaṁ viprakrānte bhikṣusaṁghe parinirvāyām || yan nv ahaṁ tata ekatyā vedanā vīryeṇa pratiprasrabhya sarvanimittānām amanasikārād ānimittaṁ cetaḥsamādhiṁ kāyena sākṣīkṛtvopasaṁpadya vihareyam ||

Wal 14.6 atha bhagavān tata ekatyā vedanā vīryeṇa pratiprasrabhya sarvanimittānām amanasikārād animittaṁ cetaḥsamādhiṁ kāyena sākṣīkṛtvopasaṁpadya vyahārṣīt || tena tathāgatasya kṣemaṇīyatarañ cābhūd yāpanīyatarañ ca ||

Wal 14.7 athāyuṣmān ānandaḥ sāyāhne pratisaṁlayanād vyutthāya yena bhagavāṁs tenopajagāma || upetya bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvaikānte ’sthāt ||

Wal 14.8 ekāntasthita āyuṣmān ānando bhagavantam idam avocat ||

Wal 14.9 api me bhadanta m. … lapante bhagavata imam evaṁ .r … āśvāsamātram || na tāvad bhagavān parinirvāsyati yāvad bhagavān bhikṣusaṁgh. …

Wal 14.10 yasyānandaivaṁ syāt || mamāsti bhikṣusaṁghaḥ || ahaṁ bhikṣusaṁghaṁ parihariṣyāmīti …

Wal 14.11 mama khalv ānanda naivaṁ bhavati || mamāsti bhikṣusaṁghaḥ || ahaṁ bhikṣusaṁghaṁ parihariṣyāmīti …

Wal 14.12 …

Wal 14.13 tadyathā catvāri smṛtyupasthānāni catvāri samyakprahāṇāni catvāra ṛddhipādāḥ pañcendriyāṇi pañca balāni sapta bodhyaṅgāny āryāṣṭāṅgo mārgaḥ ||

Wal 14.14 na tatrānanda tathāgatasya dharmeṣv ācāryamuṣṭir yaṁ tathāgataḥ praticchādayitavyaṁ manyeta || kaccin me pare na vidyur iti ||

Wal 14.15 utpannaḥ kadāpi tathāgatasya khara ābādhaḥ pragāḍhā vedanā māraṇāntikā ||

Wal 14.16 tasya ma etad abhavat || utpanno me khara ābādhaḥ pragāḍhā vedanā māraṇāntikā viprakrāntaś ca bhikṣusaṁghaḥ ||

Wal 14.17 na mama pratirūpaṁ syād yad ahaṁ viprakrānte bhikṣusaṁghe parinirvāyām || yan nv ahaṁ tata ekatyā vedanā vīryeṇa pratiprasrabhya sarvanimittānām amanasikārād animittaṁ cetaḥsamādhiṁ kāyena sākṣīkṛtvopasaṁpadya vihareyam ||

Wal 14.18 so ’haṁ tata ekatyā vedanā vīryeṇa pratiprasrabhya sarvanimittānām amanasikārād animittaṁ cetaḥsamādhiṁ kāyena sākṣīkṛtvopasaṁpadya vyahārṣam || tena tathāgatasya kṣemaṇīyatarañ cābhūd yāpanīyatarañ ca ||

Wal 14.19 punar aparam ānanda tathāgato vṛddho jīrṇatāṁ prāpto ’śītike vayasi vartate dvaidhāniśrayeṇa yāpyate || tadyathā jīrṇaṁ śakaṭaṁ dvaidhāniśrayeṇa yāpyata evam eva tathāgato vṛddho jīrnatāṁ prāpto ’śītike vayasi vartate dvaidhāniśrayeṇa yāpyate ||

Wal 14.20 mā tasmāt tvam ānanda śoca mā klāma || kasmād eva tat || kuta etal labhyaṁ yat taj jātaṁ bhūtaṁ kṛtaṁ saṁskṛtaṁ vedayitaṁ pratītyasamutpannaṁ kṣayadharmaṁ vyayadharmaṁ virodhadharmaṁ pralokadharmaṁ na prarujyate || nedaṁ sthānaṁ vidyate ||

Wal 14.21 prāg eva bhikṣavo mayākhyātaṁ sarvair iṣṭaiḥ kāntaiḥ priyair manāpair nānābhāvo bhaviṣyati vinābhāvo viprayogo visaṁyogaḥ ||

Wal 14.22 tasmād ānandaitarhi mama vātyayād ātmadvīpair vihartavyam ātmaśaraṇair dharmadvīpair dharmaśaraṇair ananyadvīpair ananyaśaraṇaiḥ || tat kasmād dhetoḥ ||

Wal 14.23 ye kecid ānandaitarhi mama vātyayād ātmadvīpā ātmaśaraṇā dharmadvīpā dharmaśaraṇā ananyadvīpā ananyaśaraṇās te ’graṁ bhaviṣyanti yaduta mama śrāvakāṇāṁ śikṣākāmānāṁ ||

Wal 14.24 kathaṁ cānanda bhikṣur ātmadvīpo bhavaty ātmaśaraṇo dharmadvīpo dharmaśaraṇo ’nanyadvīpo ’nanyaśaraṇaḥ ||

Wal 14.25 iha bhikṣur adhyātmaṁ kāye kāyānupaśyī viharaty ātāpī saṁprajānaḥ smṛtimān vinīyābhidhyā loke daurmanasyam || bahirdhā kāye ’dhyātmabahirdhā kāye ’dhyātmaṁ vedanāsu bahirdhā vedanāsv adhyātmabahirdhā vedanāsv adhyātmaṁ citte bahirdhā citte ’dhyātmabahirdhā citte ’dhyātmaṁ dharmeṣu bahirdhā dharmeṣv adhyātmabahirdhā dharmeṣu dharmānupaśyī viharaty ātāpī saṁprajānaḥ smṛtimān vinīyābhidhyā loke daurmanasyam ||

Wal 14.26 evaṁ hi bhikṣur ātmadvīpo bhavaty ātmaśaraṇo dharmadvīpo dharmaśaraṇo ’nanyadvīpo ’nanyaśaraṇaḥ ||

Hier im Tib. Uddāna

Wal 15.1 tatra bhagavān āyuṣmantam ānandam āmantrayate ||

Wal 15.2 āgamayānanda yena vaiśālī ||

Wal 15.3 evaṁ bhadantety āyuṣmān ānando bhagavataḥ pratyaśrauṣīt ||

Wal 15.4 atha bhagavān vṛjiṣu janapadeṣu caryāṁ caran vaiśālīm anuprāpto vaiśālyāṁ viharati markaṭahradatīre kūṭāgāraśālāyām ||

Wal 15.5 atha bhagavān pūrvāhṇe nivasya pātracīvaram ādāya vaiśālīṁ piṇḍāya prāviśad āyuṣmatānandena paścācchramaṇena ||

Wal 15.6 atha bhagavān vaiśālīṁ piṇḍāya caritvā kṛtabhaktakṛtyaḥ paścādbhaktapiṇḍapātaḥpratikrāntaḥ ||

Wal 15.7 pātracīvaraṁ pratiśamayya yena cāpālaṁ caityaṁ tenopajagāma || upetyānyataraṁ vṛkṣamūlaṁ niśritya niṣaṇṇo divāvihārāya ||

Wal 15.8 tatra bhagavān āyuṣmantam ānandam āmantrayate ||

Wal 15.9 ramaṇīyānanda vaiśālī vṛjibhūmiś cāpālaṁ caityaṁ saptāmrakaṁ bahupattrakaṁ gautamanyagrodhaḥ śālavanaṁ dhurānikṣepaṇaṁ mallānāṁ makuṭabandhanaṁ caityam || citro jaṁbudvīpo madhuraṁ jīvitaṁ manuṣyāṇām ||

Wal 15.10 yasya kasyacic catvāra ṛddhipādā āsevitā bhāvitā bahulīkṛtā ākāṁkṣamāṇaḥ sa kalpaṁ vā tiṣṭhet kalpāvaśeṣaṁ vā || tathāgatasyānanda catvāra ṛddhipādā āsevitā bhāvitā bahulīkṛtāḥ || ākāṁkṣamāṇas tathāgataḥ kalpaṁ vā tiṣṭhet kalpāvaśeṣaṁ vā ||

Wal 15.11 evam ukta āyuṣmān ānandas tūṣṇīm abhūt || dvir api trir api bhagavān āyuṣmantam ānandam āmantrayate ||

Wal 15.12 ramaṇīyānanda vaiśālī vṛjibhūmiś cāpālaṁ caityaṁ saptāmrakaṁ bahupattrakaṁ gautamanyagrodhaḥ śālavanaṁ dhurānikṣepaṇaṁ mallānāṁ makuṭabandhanaṁ caityam || citro jaṁbudvīpo madhuraṁ jīvitaṁ manuṣyāṇām ||

Wal 15.13 yasya kasyacic catvāra ṛddhipādā āsevitā bhāvitā bahulīkṛtā ākāṁkṣamāṇaḥ sa kalpaṁ vā tiṣṭhet kalpāvaśeṣaṁ vā || tathāgatasyānanda catvāra ṛddhipādā āsevitā bhāvitā bahulīkṛtāḥ || ākāṁkṣamāṇas tathāgataḥ kalpaṁ vā tiṣṭhet kalpāvaśeṣaṁ vā ||

Wal 15.14 dvir api trir apy āyuṣmān ānandas tūṣṇīm ||

Wal 15.15 atha bhagavata etad abhavat || sphuṭo batāyam ānando bhikṣur māreṇa pāpīyasā yatredānīṁ yāvat trir apy audārike avabhāsanimitte prāviṣkriyamāṇe na śaknoti tannimittam ājñātuṁ yathāpi tataḥ sphuṭo māreṇa pāpīyasā ||

Wal 15.16 iti viditvāyuṣmantam ānandam āmantrayate ||

Wal 15.17 gacchānandānyataravṛkṣamūlaṁ niśritya vihara mā ubhāv apy ākīrṇavihāriṇau bhaviṣyāvaḥ ||

Wal 15.18 evaṁ bhadantety āyuṣmān ānando bhagavataḥ pratiśrutyānyatamavṛkṣamūlaṁ niśritya niṣaṇṇo divāvihārāya ||

Wal 16.1 sa māraḥ pāpīyān yena bhagavāṁs tenopasaṁkrāntaḥ || upetya bhagavatpādau śirasā vanditvaikānte ’sthāt || ekāntasthito māraḥ pāpīyān bhagavantam idam avocat ||

Wal 16.2 parinirvāhi bhagavan parinirvāṇasamayaḥ sugatasya ||

Wal 16.3

Wal 16.4 kasmāt tvaṁ pāpīyann evaṁ vadasi || parinirvāhi bhagavan parinirvāṇasamayaḥ sugatasya ||

Wal 16.5 eko ’yaṁ bhadanta samayaḥ || bhagavān uruvilvāyāṁ viharati nadyā nairañjanāyās tīre bodhimūle ’cirābhisaṁbuddhaḥ || so ’haṁ yena bhagavāṁs tenopasaṁkrāntaḥ ||

Wal 16.6 upetya bhagavantam evaṁ vadāmi || parinirvāhi bhagavan parinirvāṇasamayaḥ sugatasya ||

Wal 16.7 bhagavān evam āha ||

Wal 16.8 na tāvat pāpīyan parinirvāsyāmi yāvan na me śrāvakāḥ paṇḍitā bhaviṣyanti vyaktā medhāvinaḥ || alam utpannotpannānāṁ parapravādināṁ saha dharmeṇa nigrahītāraḥ || alaṁ svasya vādasya paryavadātāro bhikṣavo bhikṣuṇya upāsakā upāsikā vaistārikaṁ ca me brahmacaryaṁ cariṣyanti bahujanyaṁ pṛthubhūtaṁ yāvad devamanuṣyebhyaḥ samyaksaṁprakāśitam ||

Wal 16.9 etarhi bhadanta bhagavataḥ śrāvakāḥ paṇḍitā vyaktā medhāvinaḥ || alam utpannotpannānāṁ parapravādināṁ saha dharmeṇa nigrahītāraḥ svasya vādasya paryavadātāro bhikṣavo bhikṣuṇya upāsakā upāsikā vaistārikaṁ ca te brahmacaryaṁ bāhujanyaṁ pṛthubhūtaṁ yāvad devamanuṣyebhyaḥ samyaksaṁprakāśitam ||

Wal 16.10 tasmād aham evaṁ vadāmi parinirvāhi bhagavan parinirvāṇasamayaḥ sugatasya ||

Wal 16.11 alpotsukas tvaṁ pāpīyan bhava na cirasyedānīṁ tathāgatasya trayāṇāṁ māsānām atyayād anupadhiśeṣe nirvāṇadhātau parinirvāṇaṁ bhaviṣyati ||

Wal 16.12 atha mārasya pāpīyasa etad abhavat || parinirvāsyate śramaṇo gautama iti viditvā hṛṣṭas tuṣṭa udagraḥ prītisaumanasyajātas tatraivāntarhitaḥ ||

Wal 16.13 atha bhagavata etad abhavat || yan nv ahaṁ tadrūpān ṛddhyabhisaṁskārān abhisaṁskuryāṁ yathā samāhite citte jīvitasaṁskārān adhiṣṭhāyāyuḥsaṁskārān utsṛjeyam ||

Wal 16.14 atha bhagavāṁs tadrūpān ṛddhyabhisaṁskārān abhisaṁskaroti yathā samāhite citte jīvitasaṁskārān adhiṣṭhāyāyuḥsaṁskārān utsṛjati || samanantarotsṛṣṭāyuḥsaṁskāreṣv atyarthaṁ tasmin samaye mahāpṛthivīcālaś cābhūd ulkāpātā diśodāhā antarīkṣe devadundubhayo ’bhinadanti ||

Wal 16.15 atha bhagavāṁs tasmāt samādher vyutthāya tasyāṁ velāyāṁ gāthāṁ babhāṣe ||

tulyam atulyaṁ ca saṁbhavaṁ
bhavasaṁskāram apotsṛjan muniḥ ||
adhyātmarataḥ samāhito
hy abhinat kośam ivāṇḍasaṁbhavaḥ |

Wal 17.1 athāyuṣmān ānando yena bhagavāṁs tenopajagāma || upetya bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvaikānte ’sthāt || ekāntasthita āyuṣmān ānando bhagavantam idam avocat ||

Wal 17.2 ko bhadanta hetuḥ kaḥ pratyayo yenaitarhy abhūn mahāpṛthivīcāla ulkāpātā diśodāhā antarīkṣe devadundubhayo ’bhinadanti ||

Wal 17.3 aṣṭāv ime hetavo ’ṣṭau pratyayā mahataḥ pṛthivīcālasya || katame ’ṣṭau ||

Wal 17.4 iyaṁ mahāpṛthivy apsu pratiṣṭhitā || āpo vāyau pratiṣṭhitā vāyur ākāśe pratiṣṭhitaḥ || bhavaty ānanda samayo yad ākāśe viṣamā vāyavo vānty āpaḥ kṣobhayanti || āpaḥ kṣubdhāḥ pṛthivīṁ cālayanti ||

Wal 17.5 ayaṁ prathamo hetuḥ prathamaḥ pratyayo mahataḥ pṛthivīcālasya ||

Wal 17.6 punar aparaṁ bhikṣur maharddhiko bhavati mahānubhāvaḥ sa parīttāṁ pṛthivīsaṁjñām adhitiṣṭhaty apramāṇāṁ cāpsaṁjñāṁ sa ākāṁkṣamāṇaḥ pṛthivīṁ cālayati ||

Wal 17.7 bhikṣuṇī devatā vā maharddhikā bhavati mahānubhāvā sā parīttāṁ pṛthivīsaṁjñām adhitiṣṭhaty apramāṇāṁ cāpsaṁjñām ākāṁkṣamāṇā pṛthivīṁ cālayati ||

Wal 17.8 ayaṁ dvitīyo hetur dvitīyaḥ pratyayo mahataḥ pṛthivīcālasya ||

Wal 17.9 punar aparaṁ yasmin samaye bodhisatvas tuṣitād devanikāyāc cyutvā mātuḥ kukṣāv avakrāmaty atyarthaṁ tasmin samaye mahāpṛthivīcālaś ca bhavati sarvaś cāyaṁ loka udāreṇāvabhāsena sphuṭo bhavanti ||

Wal 17.10 api tā lokasya lokāntarikā andhatamā andhakāratamisrā yatremau sūryācandramasāv evaṁmaharddhikāv evaṁmahānubhāvāv ābhayābhāṁ na pratyanubhavatas tā api tasmin samaye udāreṇāvabhāsena sphuṭā bhavati ||

Wal 17.11 tatra ye satvā upapannās te tayābhayānyonyaṁ satvaṁ dṛṣṭvā saṁjānante || anye ’pi bhavantaḥ satvā ihopapannāḥ || anye ’pi bhavantaḥ satvā ihopapannāḥ ||

Wal 17.12 ayaṁ tṛtīyo hetus tṛtīyaḥ pratyayo mahataḥ pṛthivīcālasya ||

Wal 17.13 punar aparaṁ yasmin samaye bodhisatvo mātuḥ kukṣer niṣkrāmaty atyarthaṁ tasmin samaye mahāpṛthivīcālaś ca bhavati pūrvavad yāvad anye ’pi bhavantaḥ satvā ihopapannāḥ ||

Wal 17.14 ayaṁ caturtho hetuś caturthaḥ pratyayo mahataḥ pṛthivīcālasya ||

Wal 17.15 punar aparaṁ yasmin samaye bodhisatvo ’nuttarāṁ samyaksaṁbodhim adhigacchaty atyarthaṁ tasmin samaye mahāpṛthivīcālaś ca bhavati pūrvavat ||

Wal 17.16 ayaṁ pañcamo hetuḥ pañcamaḥ pratyayo mahataḥ pṛthivīcālasya ||

Wal 17.17 punar aparam ānanda yasmin samaye tathāgatas triparivartaṁ dvādaśākāraṁ dhārmyaṁ dharmacakraṁ pravartayaty atyarthaṁ tasmin samaye mahāpṛthivīcālaś ca bhavati pūrvavat ||

Wal 17.18 ayaṁ ṣaṣṭho hetuḥ ṣaṣṭhaḥ pratyayo mahataḥ pṛthivīcālasya ||

Wal 17.19 punar aparaṁ yasmin samaye tathāgato jīvitasaṁskārān adhiṣṭhāyāyuḥsaṁskārān utsṛjaty atyarthaṁ tasmin samaye mahāpṛthivīcālo bhavaty ulkāpātā diśodāhā antarīkṣe devadundubhayo ’bhinadanti ||

Wal 17.20 ayaṁ saptamo hetuḥ saptamaḥ pratyayo mahataḥ pṛthivīcālasya ||

Wal 17.21 punar aparaṁ na cirasyedānīṁ tathāgatasyānupadhiśeṣe nirvāṇadhātau parinirvāṇaṁ bhaviṣyati || atyarthaṁ tasmin samaye mahāpṛthivīcālaś ca bhavaty ulkāpātā diśodāhā antarīkṣe devadundubhayo ’bhinadanti ||

Wal 17.22 ayam aṣṭamo hetur aṣṭamaḥ pratyayo mahataḥ pṛthivīcālasya ||

Wal 18.1 athāyuṣmān ānando bhagavantam idam avocat ||

Wal 18.2 yathā khalv ahaṁ bhadanta bhagavato bhāṣitasyārtham ājānāmi bhagavataitarhi jīvitasaṁskārān adhiṣṭhāyāyuḥsaṁskārā utsṛṣṭāḥ ||

Wal 18.3 evam etad ānandaivam etad ānanda || etarhy ānanda tathāgatena jīvitasaṁskārān adhiṣṭhāyāyuḥsaṁskārā utsṛṣṭāḥ ||

Wal 18.4 saṁmukhaṁ me bhadanta bhagavato ’ntikāc chrutaṁ saṁmukham udgṛhītam || yasya kasyacic catvāra ṛddhipādā āsevitā bhāvitā bahulīkṛtā ākāṁkṣamāṇaḥ kalpam api tiṣṭhet kalpāvaśeṣam api ||

Wal 18.5 bhagavato bhadanta catvāra ṛddhipādā āsevitā bhāvitā bahulīkṛtā ākāṁkṣamāṇas tathāgatas kalpaṁ vā tiṣṭhet kalpāvaśeṣaṁ vā ||

Wal 18.6 tiṣṭhatu bhagavān kalpaṁ tiṣṭhatu sugataḥ kalpāvaśeṣam ||

Wal 18.7 tavaivānandāparādhas tavaiva duṣkṛtaṁ yas tvaṁ tathāgatasya yāvat trir apy audāre ’vabhāsanimitte prāviṣkriyamāṇe na śaknoṣi taṁ nimittaṁ prativeddhuṁ yathāpi tat sphuṭo māreṇa pāpīyasā ||

Wal 18.8 kiṁ manyasa ānanda bhāṣeta tathāgatas tāṁ vācaṁ yā syād dvaidhavipākyā || no bhadanta ||

Wal 18.9 sādhu sādhv ānanda || asthānam anavakāśo yat tahāgatas tāṁ vācaṁ bhāṣeta yā syād dvaidhavipākyā ||

Wal 19.1 gaccha tvam ānanda yāvanto bhikṣavaś cāpālaṁ caityam upaniśritya viharanti tān sarvān upasthānaśālāyāṁ sannipātaya ||

Wal 19.2 evaṁ bhadanta || āyuṣmān ānando bhagavataḥ pratiśrutya yāvanto bhikṣavaś cāpālaṁ caityam upaniśritya viharanti tān sarvān upasthānaśālāyāṁ sannipātya yena bhagavāṁs tenopasaṁkrāntaḥ || upasaṁkramya bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvaikānte ’sthāt ||

Wal 19.3 ekāntasthita āyuṣmān ānando bhagavantam idam avocat ||

Wal 19.4 yāvanto bhadanta bhikṣavaś cāpālaṁ caityam upaniśritya viharanti sarve ta upasthānaśālāyāṁ niṣaṇṇāḥ sannipatitāḥ || yasyedānīṁ bhagavān kālaṁ manyate ||

Wal 19.5 atha bhagavān yenopasthānaśālā tenopasaṁkrāntaḥ || upasaṁkramya purastād bhikṣusaṁghasya prajñapta evāsane nyaṣīdat || niṣadya bhagavān bhikṣūn āmantrayate sma ||

Wal 19.6 anityā bhikṣavaḥ sarvasaṁskārā adhruvā anāśvāsikā vipariṇāmadharmāṇo yāvad alam eva bhikṣavaḥ sarvasaṁskārān saṁskaritum alaṁ virantum ||

Wal 19.7 tasmāt tarhi bhikṣavo ye te dharmā dṛṣṭadharmahitāya saṁvartante dṛṣṭadharmasukhāya saṁparāyahitāya saṁparāyasukhāya te bhikṣubhir udgṛhya paryavāpya tathā tathā dhārayitavyā grāhayitavyā vācayitavyā yathedaṁ brahmacaryaṁ cirasthitikaṁ syāt tad bhaviṣyati bahujanahitāya bahujanasukhāya lokānukampāyārthāya hitāya sukhāya devamanuṣyāṇāṁ ||

Wal 19.8 katame te dharmā dṛṣṭadharmahitāya saṁvartante dṛṣṭadharmasukhāya saṁparāyahitāya saṁparāyasukhāya te bhikṣubhir udgṛhya pūrvavad yāvad devamanuṣyāṇām ||

Wal 19.9 tadyathā catvāri smṛtyupasthānāni catvāri samyakprahāṇāni catvāra ṛddhipādāḥ pañcendriyāṇi pañca balāni sapta bodhyaṅgāny āryāṣṭāṅgo mārgaḥ ||

Wal 19.10 ime te dharmā dṛṣṭadharmahitāya saṁvartante pūrvavad yāvad devamanuṣyāṇām ||

Wal 20.1 tatra bhagavān āyuṣmantam ānandam āmantrayate ||

Wal 20.2 āgamayānanda yena kuṣṭhagrāmakaḥ ||

Wal 20.3 evaṁ bhadantety āyuṣmān ānando bhagavataḥ pratyaśrauṣīt ||

Wal 20.4 bhagavān vaiśālīsāmantakenātikraman dakṣiṇena sarvakāyena nāgāvalokitenāvalokayati ||

Wal 20.5 adrākṣīd āyuṣmān ānando bhagavantaṁ dakṣiṇena sarvakāyena nāgāvalokitena vyavalokayantaṁ dṛṣṭvā punar bhagavantam idam avocat ||

Wal 20.6 nāhetv apratyayaṁ bhadanta tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksaṁbuddhā nāgāvalokitam avalokayanti || ko bhadanta hetuḥ kaḥ pratyayo nāgāvalokitasya ||

Wal 20.7 evam etad ānandaivam etad ānanda || nāhetv apratyayaṁ tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksaṁbuddhā dakṣiṇena sarvakāyena nāgāvalokitenāvalokayanti ||

Wal 20.8 idam ānanda tathāgatasya vaiśālyāḥ paścimaṁ darśanaṁ na bhūya iha saṁbuddho vaiśālīm āgamiṣyati || parinirvāṇāya gamiṣyati mallānām upavartanaṁ yamakaśālavanam ||

Wal 20.9 athānyataro bhikṣus tasyāṁ velāyāṁ gāthāṁ babhāṣe ||

Wal 20.10 idam apaścimakaṁ nātha
vaiśālyās tava darśanam ||
na bhūyaḥ sugato buddho
vaiśālīm āgamiṣyati ||
nirvāṇāya prayāto ’yaṁ
mallānām upavartane |

Wal 21.1 atha bhagavān vṛjiṣu janapadeṣu caryāṁ caraṅ kuṣṭhagrāmakam anuprāptaḥ kuṣṭhagrāmake viharaty uttareṇa grāmasya śiṁśapāvane ||

Wal 21.2 tatra bhagavān bhikṣūn āmantrayate |

Wal 21.3 itīmāni bhikṣavaḥ śīlāni || ayaṁ samādhiḥ || iyaṁ prajñā || śīlaprabhāvitaḥ samādhiś cirasthitiko bhavati || prajñāparibhāvitaṁ cittaṁ samyag eva vimucyate rāgadveṣamohebhyaḥ ||

Wal 21.4 evaṁ samyaksuvimuktacitta āryaśrāvakaḥ samyag eva prajānāti ||

Wal 21.5 kṣīṇā me jātir uṣitaṁ brahmacaryaṁ kṛtaṁ karaṇīyaṁ nāparam asmād bhavaṁ prajānāmi ||

Hier im Tib. und Skt. Uddāna; cf. MPS p. 495:

kuṣṭha gaṇḍa āmra ca
jambu śūrpa tūla hasti ca ||
grāmau ca vṛjimallau
bhoganagarakaṁ tathā |

Wal 21.6 yathā kuṣṭhagrāmaka evaṁ gaṇḍagrāmako droṇagrāmakaḥ śūrpagrāmaka āmragrāmako jambugrāmako hastigrāmakaḥ ||

Wal 21.7 vṛjigrāmakān mallagrāmakād bhoganagarakam anuprāptaḥ || bhoganagarake viharaty uttareṇa grāmasya śiṁśapāvane ||

Wal 21.8 tatra bhagavān bhikṣūn āmantrayate ||

Wal 21.9 itīmāni bhikṣavaḥ śīlāni pūrvavad yāvad nāparam asmād bhāvaṁ prajānāmi ||

Wal 22.1 tena khalu samayena mahāpṛthivīcālaś cābhūd ulkāpātā diśodāhā antarīkṣe devadundubhayo ’bhinadanti ||

Wal 22.2 athāyuṣmān ānandaḥ sāyāhne pratisaṁlayanād vyutthāya yena bhagavāṁs tenopajagāma || upetya bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvaikānte ’sthāt ||

Wal 22.3 ekāntasthita āyuṣmān ānando bhagavantam idam avocat ||

Wal 22.4 ko bhadanta hetuḥ kaḥ pratyayo yenaitarhy abhūd mahāpṛthivīcāla ulkāpātā diśodāhā antarīkṣe devadundubhayo ’bhinadanti ||

Wal 22.5 traya ime ānanda hetavas trayaḥ pratyayā mahataḥ pṛthivīcālasya ||

Wal 22.6 katame trayaḥ ||

Wal 22.7 iyaṁ mahāpṛthivy apsu pratiṣṭhitā pūrvavad yāvac cālayanti ||

Wal 22.8 ayaṁ prathamo hetuḥ prathamaḥ pratyayo mahataḥ pṛthivīcālasya ||

Wal 22.9 punar aparaṁ bhikṣur maharddhiko bhavati pūrvavad yāvac cālayati ||

Wal 22.10 Nur Tibetisch.

Wal 22.11 ayaṁ dvitīyo hetur dvitīyaḥ pratyayo mahataḥ pṛthivīcālasya ||

Wal 22.12 punar aparaṁ na cirasyedānīṁ tathāgatasyānupadhiśeṣe nirvāṇadhātau parinirvāṇaṁ bhaviṣyati || atyarthaṁ tasmin samaye mahāpṛthivīcālaś ca bhavaty ulkāpātā diśodāhā antarīkṣe devadundubhayo ’bhinadanti ||

Wal 22.13 ayaṁ tṛtīyo hetus tṛtīyaḥ pratyayo mahataḥ pṛthivīcālasya ||

Wal 23.1 athāyuṣmān ānando bhagavantam idam avocat ||

Wal 23.2 āscaryādbhutadharmasamanvāgatās tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksaṁbuddhāḥ || yatredānīṁ na cirasya tathāgatasyānupadhiśeṣe nirvāṇadhātau parinirvāṇaṁ bhaviṣyaty atyarthaṁ tasmin samaye mahāpṛthivīcālaś ca bhavaty ulkāpātā diśodāhā antarīkṣe devadundubhayo ’bhinadanti ||

Wal 23.3 evam etad ānanda evam etad ānanda || āścaryādbhutadharmasamanvāgatā eva tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksaṁbuddhāḥ ||

Wal 23.4 abhijānāmi khalu punar aham anekaśataṁ kṣatriyapariṣadaṁ darśanāyopasaṁkramitum upasaṁkrāntasya ca me yādṛśas teṣām ārohapariṇāho bhavati mamāpi tādṛśa ārohapariṇāho bhavati || yādṛśī teṣāṁ varṇapuṣkalatā bhavati mamāpi tādṛśī varṇapuṣkalatā bhavati || yādṛśī teṣāṁ svaraguptir bhavati mamāpi tādṛśī svaraguptir bhavati ||

Wal 23.5 te yam arthaṁ mantrayanty aham api tam arthaṁ mantrayāmi || te yam arthaṁ na mantrayanty aham api tam arthaṁ na mantrayāmi || uttare vai tān dhārmyā kathayā sandarśayāmi samādāpayāmi samuttejayāmi saṁpraharṣayāmi tato ’ntardhāpayāmi || antarhitasya me na jānanti ka eṣa antarhito devo vā manuṣyo vā ||

Wal 23.6 evam api brāhmaṇapariṣadaṁ gṛhapatipariṣadaṁ śramaṇapariṣadaṁ cāturmahārājikān devāṁs trāyastriṁśān yāmāṁs tuṣitān nirmāṇaratīn parinirmitavaśavartino brahmakāyikān brahmapāriṣadyān brahmapurohitān mahābrahmaṇaḥ parīttābhān apramāṇābhān ābhāsvarān parīttaśubhān apramāṇaśubhāñ śubhakṛtsnān anabhrakān puṇyaprasavān bṛhatphalān abṛhān atapān sudṛśān sudarśanān akaniṣṭhān devān darśanāyopasaṁkramitum

Wal 23.7 upasaṁkrāntasya ca me yādṛśas teṣām ārohapariṇāho bhavati pūrvavad yāvad devo vā manuṣyo vā ||

Wal 23.8 evam āścaryādbhutadharmasamanvāgatās tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksaṁbuddhāḥ ||

Wal 24.1 tatra bhagavān āyuṣmantam ānandam āmantrayate ||

Wal 24.2 tasmāt tarhi ta ānanda bhikṣubhiḥ sūtrāntapratisaraṇair bhavitavyaṁ na pudgalapratisaraṇaiḥ ||

Wal 24.3 kathaṁ bhikṣuḥ sūtrāntapratisaraṇo bhavati na pudgalapratisaraṇaḥ ||

Wal 24.4 ihānanda bhikṣur āgacchet sa evaṁ vadet ||

Wal 24.5 saṁmukhaṁ me bhagavato ’ntikāc chrutaṁ saṁmukham udgṛhītam ayaṁ dharmo ’yaṁ vinaya idaṁ śāstuḥ śāsanam ||

Wal 24.6 tasya bhikṣavas tan notsāhayitavyaṁ nāvasādayitavyam || anutsāhayitvānavasādayitvā śrotram avadhāya tāni padavyaṁjanāny udgṛhya sūtre ’vatārayitavyaṁ vinaye saṁdarśayitavyaṁ || yadi sūtre ’vatāryamāṇā vinaye saṁdarśyamānāḥ sūtre nāvataranti vinaye na saṁdṛśyante dharmatāṁ ca vilomayanti sa evaṁ syād vacanīyaḥ ||

Wal 24.7 addhāyuṣmann ime dharmā na bhagavatā bhāṣitāḥ || āyuṣmatā vā ime dharmā durgṛhītās tathā hīme dharmāḥ sūtre ’vatāryamāṇā vinaye saṁdarśyamānāḥ sūtre nāvataranti vinaye na saṁdṛśyante dharmatāṁ ca vilomayanti ||

Wal 24.8 nāyaṁ dharmo nāyaṁ vinayo nedaṁ śāstuḥ śāsanam iti viditvā chorayitavyāḥ ||

Wal 24.9 punar aparam ānanda bhikṣur āgacchet sa evaṁ vadet ||

Wal 24.10 amuṣminn āvāse mahān bhikṣusaṁghaḥ prativasati sasthaviraḥ sapramokṣaḥ ||

Wal 24.11 saṁmukhaṁ me tasya mahato bhikṣusaṁghasyāntikāc chrutaṁ saṁmukham udgṛhītam ayaṁ dharmo ’yaṁ vinaya idaṁ śāstuḥ śāsanaṁ ||

Wal 24.12 tasya bhikṣavas tan notsāhayitavyaṁ nāvasādayitavyam || anutsāhayitvānavasādayitvā śrotram avadhāya tāni padavyaṁjanāny udgṛhya sūtre ’vatārayitavyaṁ vinaye saṁdarśayitavyaṁ || yadi sūtre ’vatāryamāṇā vinaye saṁdarśyamānāḥ sūtre nāvataranti vinaye na saṁdṛśyante dharmatāṁ ca vilomayanti sa evaṁ syād vacanīyaḥ ||

Wal 24.13 addhāyuṣmaṁs tena mahatā bhikṣusaṁghena dharmasaṁjñinā ca vinayasaṁjñinā cādharmaś cāvinayaś ca bhāṣitaḥ || āyuṣmatā vā ime dharmā durgṛhītās tathā hīme dharmāḥ sūtre ’vatāryamāṇā vinaye saṁdarśyamānāḥ sūtre nāvataranti vinaye na saṁdṛśyante dharmatāṁ ca vilomayanti ||

Wal 24.14 nāyaṁ dharmo nāyaṁ vinayo nedaṁ śāstuḥ śāsanam iti viditvā chorayitavyāḥ ||

Wal 24.15 punar aparam ānanda bhikṣur āgacchet sa evaṁ vadet ||

Wal 24.16 amuṣminn āvāse saṁbahulā bhikṣavaḥ prativasanti sūtradharā vinayadharā mātṛkādharāḥ ||

Wal 24.17 saṁmukhaṁ me teṣāṁ saṁbahulānāṁ bhikṣūṇām antikāc chrutaṁ saṁmukham udgṛhītam ayaṁ dharmo ’yaṁ vinaya idaṁ śāstuḥ śāsanaṁ

Wal 24.18 tasya bhikṣavas tan notsāhayitavyaṁ pūrvavad yāvat sa evaṁ syād vacanīyaḥ ||

Wal 24.19 addhāyuṣmaṁs tair bhikṣubhir dharmasaṁjñibhiś ca vinayasaṁjñibhiś cādharmaś cāvinayaś ca bhāṣitaḥ || pūrvavad

Wal 24.20 yāvad iti viditvā chorayitavyāḥ ||

Wal 24.21 punar aparam ānanda bhikṣur āgacchet sa evaṁ vadet ||

Wal 24.22 amuṣminn āvāse bhikṣuḥ prativasati sthaviraḥ … = 24.45

Wal 24.23 saṁmukhaṁ me tasya bhikṣor antikāc chrutaṁ saṁmukham udgṛhītam ayaṁ dharmo ’yaṁ vinaya idaṁ śāstuḥ śāsanaṁ ||

Wal 24.24 tasya bhikṣavas tan notsāhayitavyaṁ pūrvavad yāvat sa evaṁ syād vacanīyaḥ ||

Wal 24.25 addhāyuṣmaṁs tena bhikṣuṇā dharmasaṁjñinā ca vinayasaṁjñinā cādharmaś cāvinayaś ca bhāṣitaḥ || pūrvavad

Wal 24.26 yāvad iti viditvā chorayitavyāḥ ||

Wal 24.27 punar aparam ānanda bhikṣur āgacchet sa evaṁ vadet ||

Wal 24.28 saṁmukhaṁ me bhagavato ’ntikāc chrutaṁ saṁmukham udgṛhītam ayaṁ dharmo ’yaṁ vinaya idaṁ śāstuḥ śāsanam ||

Wal 24.29 tasya bhikṣavas tan notsāhayitavyaṁ nāvasādayitavyam || anutsāhayitvānavasādayitvā śrotram avadhāya tāni padavyañjanāny udgṛhya sūtre ’vatārayitavyaṁ vinaye sandarśayitavyaṁ || yadi sūtre ’vatāryamāṇā vinaye sandarśyamānāḥ sūtre ’vataranti vinaye saṁdṛśyante dharmatāṁ ca na vilomayanti sa evaṁ syād vacanīyaḥ ||

Wal 24.30 addhāyuṣmann ime dharmā bhagavatā bhāṣitāḥ || āyuṣmatā ceme dharmāḥ sugṛhītās tathā hīme dharmāḥ sūtre ’vatāryamāṇā vinaye saṁdarśyamānāḥ sūtre ’vataranti vinaye saṁdṛśyante dharmatāṁ ca na vilomayanti ||

Wal 24.31 ayaṁ dharmo ’yaṁ vinaya idaṁ śāstuḥ śāsanam iti viditvā dhārayitavyāḥ ||

Wal 24.32 punar aparam ānanda bhikṣur āgacchet sa evaṁ vadet ||

Wal 24.33 amuṣminn āvāse mahān bhikṣusaṁghaḥ prativasati sasthaviraḥ sapramokṣaḥ ||

Wal 24.34 saṁmukhaṁ me tasya mahato bhikṣusaṁghasyāntikāc chrutaṁ saṁmukham udgṛhītam ayaṁ dharmo ’yaṁ vinaya idaṁ śāstuḥ śāsanam ||

Wal 24.35 tasya bhikṣavas tan notsāhayitavyaṁ pūrvavad yāvat sa evaṁ syād vacanīyaḥ ||

Wal 24.36 addhāyuṣmaṁs tena mahatā bhikṣusaṁghena dharmasaṁjñinā vinayasaṁjñinātra dharmaś ca vinayaś ca bhāṣitaḥ || āyuṣmatā ceme dharmāḥ sugṛhītās tathā hīme dharmāḥ sūtre ’vatāryamāṇā vinaye saṁdarśyamānāḥ sūtre ’vataranti vinaye na saṁdṛśyante dharmatāñ ca na vilomayanti ||

Wal 24.37 ayaṁ dharmo ’yaṁ vinaya idaṁ śāstuḥ śāsanam iti viditvā dhārayitavyāḥ ||

Wal 24.38 punar aparam ānanda bhikṣur āgacchet sa evaṁ vadet ||

Wal 24.39 amuṣminn āvāse saṁbahulā bhikṣavaḥ prativasanti sūtradharā vinayadharā mātṛkādharāḥ ||

Wal 24.40 saṁmukhaṁ me teṣāṁ saṁbahulānāṁ bhikṣūṇām antikāc chrutaṁ saṁmukham udgṛhītam ayaṁ dharmo ’yaṁ vinaya idaṁ śāstuḥ śāsanaṁ ||

Wal 24.41 tasya bhikṣavas tan notsāhayitavyaṁ pūrvavad yāvat sa evaṁ syād vacanīyaḥ ||

Wal 24.42 addhāyuṣmaṁs tair bhikṣubhir dharmasaṁjñibhiś ca vinayasaṁjñibhiś ca dharmaś ca vinayaś ca bhāṣitaḥ || āyuṣmatā ceme dharmāḥ sugṛhītās tathā hīme dharmāḥ sūtre ’vatāryamāṇā pūrvavad yāvad

Wal 24.43 ayaṁ dharmo ’yaṁ vinaya idaṁ śāstuḥ śāsanam iti viditvā dhārayitavyāḥ ||

Wal 24.44 punar aparam ānanda bhikṣur āgacchet sa evaṁ vadet ||

Wal 24.45 amuṣminn āvāse bhikṣuḥ prativasati sthaviraḥ … = 24.22

Wal 24.46 saṁmukhaṁ me tasya bhikṣor antikāc chrutaṁ saṁmukham udgṛhītam ayaṁ dharmo ’yaṁ vinaya idaṁ śāstuḥ śāsanam ||

Wal 24.47 tasya bhikṣavas tan notsāhayitavyaṁ pūrvavad yāvat sa evaṁ syād vacanīyaḥ ||

Wal 24.48 addhāyuṣmaṁs tena bhikṣuṇā dharmasaṁjñinā ca vinayasaṁjñinā ca dharmaś ca vinayaś ca bhāṣitaḥ || pūrvavad

Wal 24.49 yāvad iti viditvā dhārayitavyāḥ ||

Wal 24.50 tatrānanda ye te pūrvakāś catv. … nāyaṁ dharmo nāyaṁ vinayo nedaṁ śāstuḥ śāsanam iti viditvā chorayitavyāḥ ||

Wal 24.51 tatrānanda ye te … ayaṁ dharmo ’yaṁ vinaya idaṁ śāstuḥ śāsanam iti viditvā dhārayitavyāḥ ||

Wal 24.52 evam evānanda bhikṣubhiḥ sūtrāntapratisaraṇair bhavitavyaṁ na pudgalapratisaraṇaiḥ ||

Wal 25 = Sondertext I ST.I. CT 417ff.

Wal 25.1 tatra bhagavān āyuṣmantam ānadam āmantrayate ||

Wal 25.2 āgamayānanda yena rāmagrāmakaḥ || evaṁ bhadantety āyuṣmān ānando bhagavataḥ pratyaśrauṣīt ||

Wal 25.3 atha bhagavān krauḍyeṣu janapadeṣu caryāṁ caraṁ rāmagrāmakam anuprāpto rāmagrāmake viharati …

Wal 25.4 tatra bhagavān āyuṣmantam ānandam āmantrayate ||

rāmagrāmake r. .i .. nāma krauḍyaḥ prativasati || sa tathāgatasya parinirvṛtasya rāmagrāmake śarīrastūpaṁ pratiṣṭhāpayiṣyati śarīrāṇāṁ satkārāya gurukārāya mānanāya pūjanāya arcanāya apacitaye ||

Wal 25.5 sa tathāgatasya parinirvṛtasya śarīrastūpapratiṣṭhāpanena … kalpān vinipātaṁ na gamiṣyati devāṁś ca manuṣyāṁś ca sandhāvya saṁsṛtya paścime bhave paścime nikete paścime samucchraye paścime ātmabhāvapratilambhe manuṣyatvaṁ pratilabhya … dharmacaritena keśaśmaśrūṇy avatārya kāṣāyāṇi vastrāṇy ācchādya samyag eva śraddhayāgārād anagārikāṁ pravrajya pratyekāṁ bodhiṁ sākṣīkariṣyati ||

Wal 25.6 viṣṇudvīpe ānanda śubhākṛtsno nāma brāhmaṇaḥ prativasati || so ’pi tathāgatasya parinirvṛtasya viṣṇudvīpe śarīrastūpaṁ pratiṣṭhāpya

Wal 25.7 etena śarīrastūpapratiṣṭhāpanena … kalpān vinipātaṁ na gamiṣyati devāṁś ca manuṣyāṁś ca pūrvavad yāvat pratyekāṁ bodhiṁ sākṣīkariṣyati ||

Wal 25.8 kapilavastuny ānanda … buddho nāma śākyaḥ prativasati || so ’pi tathāgatasya parinirvṛtasya kapilavastuni śarīrastūpaṁ pratiṣṭhāpya

Wal 25.9 etena śarīrastūpapratiṣṭhāpanena … kalpān vinipātaṁ na gamiṣyati devāṁś ca manuṣyāṁś ca pūrvavad yāvat pratyekāṁ bodhiṁ sākṣīkariṣyati ||

Wal 25.10 rājagṛhe ānanda rājā māgadha ajātaśatrur vaidehīputraḥ prativasati || so ’pi tathāgatasya parinirvṛtasya rājagṛhe śarīrastūpaṁ pratiṣṭhāpayiṣyati śarīrāṇāṁ satkārāya gurukārāya mānanāya pūjanāya arcanāya apacitaye ||

Wal 25.11 sa tathāgatasya parinirvṛtasya śarīrastūpapratiṣṭhāpanena … kalpān vinipātaṁ na gamiṣyati devāṁś ca manuṣyāṁś ca pūrvavad yāvat pratyekāṁ bodhiṁ sākṣīkariṣyati ||

Wal 25.12 atha bhagavāṁs tasyāṁ velāyāṁ gāthā babhāṣe ||

Wal 25.13 śataṁ sahasrāṇi suvarṇaniṣkā
jāṁbūnadā nāsya samā bhavaṁti ||
ye buddhacaityeṣu prasaṁnacittāḥ
padā vihāre samatikramaṁti |

Wal 25.14 śataṁ sahasrāṇi suvarṇapiṇḍā
jāṁbūnadā nāsya samā bhavaṁti ||
yo buddhacaityeṣu prasannacitta
āropayen mṛttikapiṇḍam ekam |

Wal 25.15 śataṁ sahasrāṇi suvarṇamūṭā
jāṁbūnadā nāsya samā bhavaṁti ||
yo buddhacaityeṣu prasannacitta
āropayen muktapuṣpasya rāśim |

Wal 25.16 śataṁ sahasrāṇi suvarṇakoṭya
jāṁbūnadā nāsya samā bhavaṁti ||
yo buddhacaityeṣu prasannacittaḥ
pradīpadānaṁ prakaroti vidvān |

Wal 25.17 śataṁ sahasrāṇi suvarṇavāhāḥ
jāṁbūnadā nāsya samā bhavaṁti ||
yo buddhacaityeṣu prasannacitto
mālāvihāraṁ prakaroti vidvān |

Wal 25.18 śataṁ sahasrāṇi suvarṇaparvatāḥ
meroḥ samā nāsya samā bhavaṁti ||
yo buddhacaityeṣu prasannacitta
āropayec chatradhvajaṁ patākam |

Wal 25.19 eṣāho dakṣiṇā proktā
aprameyā tathāgate ||
samudrakalpe saṁbuddhe
sārthavāhe anuttare |

Wal 25.20 tiṣṭhantaṁ pūjayed yaś ca
yaś cāpi parinirvṛtam ||
same cittaprasāde hi
nāsti puṇyaviśeṣatā |

Wal 25.21 na hi citte prasanne ’smim*
svalpā bhavati dakṣiṇā ||
tathāgate vā saṁbuddhe
buddhānāṁ śrāvakeṣu vā |

Wal 25.22 evaṁ hy acintitā buddhā
buddhadharmo ’py acintitaḥ ||
acintite prasādyeha
vipākaḥ syād acintitaḥ |

Wal 25.23 teṣām acintitānām
apratihatadharmacakravartīnām ||
samyaksaṁbuddhānāṁ nālaṁ
guṇapāram adhigantum |

25.24 uddānam* | Cf. Bl. 185 R 6:
.. calakalpā viṣṇudvīpaṁ kapilavastu + rājagṛhaṁ paścimaṁ jñeyam* rāmaś ca ro

Wal 26.1 tatra bhagavān āyuṣmantam ānandam āmantrayate ||

Wal 26.2 āgamayānanda yena pāpāgrāmakaḥ || evaṁ bhadantety āyuṣmān ānando bhagavataḥ pratyaśrauṣīt ||

Wal 26.3 atha bhagavān malleṣu janapadeṣv anupūrveṇa caryāṁ caran pāpām anuprāptaḥ pāpāyāṁ viharati jalūkāvanaṣaṇḍe ||

Wal 26.4 aśrauṣuḥ pāpīyakā mallā bhagavān malleṣu janapadeṣv anupūrveṇa caryāṁ caran pāpām anuprāptaḥ pāpāyāṁ viharati jalūkāvanaṣaṇḍe ||

Wal 26.5 śrutvā ca punaḥ saṁghāt saṁghaṁ pūgāt pūgaṁ saṁgamya samāgamya pāpāyā niṣkramya yena bhagavāṁs tenopajagmuḥ ||

Wal 26.6 upetya bhagavatpādau śirasā vanditvaikānte nyaṣīdan || ekāntaniṣaṇṇān bhagavān dhārmyā kathayā sandarśayati samādāpayati samuttejayati saṁpraharṣayati ||

Wal 26.7 tena khalu samayena cundaḥ karmāraputras tasmin samāje sanniṣaṇṇo ’bhūt sannipatitaḥ || atha bhagavān pāpīyakān mallān anekaparyāyeṇa dhārmyā kathayā sandarśayitvā samādāpayitvā samuttejayitvā saṁpraharṣayitvā tūṣṇīm abhūt || atha pāpīyakā mallā bhagavato bhāṣitam abhinandyānumodya bhagavatpādau śirasā vanditvā prakrāntāḥ ||

Wal 26.8 cundaḥ karmāraputras tatraivāsthāt || atha cundaḥ karmāraputro ’ciraprakrāntān pāpīyakān mallān viditvotthāyāsanād ekāṁsam uttarāsaṅgaṁ kṛtvā yena bhagavāṁs tenāñjaliṁ praṇamya bhagavantam idam avocat ||

Wal 26.9 adhivāsayatu me bhagavāñ śvo bhaktena sārdhaṁ bhikṣusaṁghena ||

Wal 26.10 adhivāsayati bhagavāñ cundasya karmāraputrasya tūṣṇīṁbhāvena ||

Wal 26.11 atha cundaḥ karmāraputro bhagavatas tūṣṇīṁbhāvenādhivāsanāṁ viditvā bhagavato bhāṣitam abhinandyānumodya bhagavatpādau śirasā vanditvā bhagavato ’ntikāt prakrāntaḥ ||

Wal 26.12 atha cundaḥ karmāraputras tām eva rātriṁ śuciṁ praṇītaṁ khādanīyabhojanīyaṁ samudānīya kālyam evotthāyāsanakāni prajñapyodakamaṇiṁ pratiṣṭhāpya bhagavato dūtena kālam ārocayati ||

Wal 26.13 samayo bho gautamo sadyo bhaktaṁ yasyedānīṁ bhavāṅ gautamaḥ kālaṁ manyate ||

Wal 26.14 atha bhagavān pūrvāhṇe nivasya pātracīvaram ādāya bhikṣusaṁghaparivṛto bhikṣusaṁghapuraskṛto yena cundasya karmāraputrasya bhaktābhisāras tenopajagāma || upetya purastād bhikṣusaṁghasya prajñapta evāsane nyaṣīdat ||

Wal 26.15 atha cundaḥ karmāraputraḥ sukhopaniṣaṇṇaṁ buddhapramukhaṁ bhikṣusaṁghaṁ viditvā bhagavantaṁ praṇītena khādanīyena lohakaroṭakāt svahastaṁ santarpayati saṁpravārayati || bhikṣusaṁghaṁ ca śucinā praṇītena khādanīyabhojanīyena svahastaṁ santarpayati saṁpravārayati ||

Wal 26.16 tena samayena anyatamaḥ pāpabhikṣur lohakaroṭakaṁ kakṣeṇāpahṛtavāṁs taṁ khalu pāpabhikṣuṁ bhagavān adrākṣīc cundaś ca buddhānubhāvena ||

Wal 26.17 atha cundaḥ karmāraputro buddhapramukhaṁ bhikṣusaṁghaṁ śucinā praṇītena khādanīyabhojanīyena svahastaṁ santarpayitvā saṁpravārayitvā bhagavantaṁ bhuktavantaṁ viditvā dhautahastam apanītapātraṁ nīcatarakam āsanaṁ gṛhītvā bhagavataḥ purato niṣadya bhagavantaṁ gāthābhir gītābhiḥ papraccha ||

Wal 26.30 dadataḥ puṇyaṁ pra + + +
